The budget for expenses has been drafted and sent to the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics for review. It is expected to be approved this week, and organization will begin immediately. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

Xiao Zhenying Arrives in Nanjing from Jiangxi 46

(Nanjing) Xiao Zhenying, representative of Song Zheyuan, arrived in Nanjing from Jiangxi, stating that his meeting with Chiang Kai-shek in Jiangxi was successful. It has now been announced that Liu Zhi, He Chengjun, and He Jian will be the bandit suppression commissioners for the border areas in Jiangxi. From now on, the encirclement and suppression of the Jiangxi bandits will be the responsibility of the three commissioners. The bandit suppression troops from the Southwest, Fujian, Guangdong, and Guangxi are already on their way and should be able to encircle southern Jiangxi soon. Chiang Kai-shek will wait for the arrangements in Jiangxi to be completed before heading north to oversee the operations. It is undecided whether he will return to Nanjing and then go north or go north from Jiangxi to Wuhan. The date of his departure north may not be far off. Song Zheyuan has not yet recovered from his back pain. In view of the urgent situation at the front, he has gone to the front line despite his illness. A telegram stated that our army has recovered Daxiaoxifengkou and has been victorious in all battles. He himself will go to Shanghai this evening to discuss important matters with various circles in Shanghai. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

Ministry of Communications Reorganizes Purchasing Committee 47

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications has reorganized the Purchasing Committee, appointing Wen Yuqing, Cheng Shifan, Mao Yike, Niu Yinguo, and others as members, and designating Wen as the chairman. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

Page 5

Current Commentary

War News - Sigh 48

In recent days, after the Japanese military announced its withdrawal, Japanese troops have been withdrawing to the east of the Shi River. Today, the commanding general of the forward troops returned to Peiping and reported at the Peiping branch that the Japanese side was withdrawing its troops, indicating that there should be no fighting on the front line. However, on the one hand, telegraphic news indicates that the fighting at Gubeikou and Xifengkou is still very fierce and frequent, and there are frequent warnings of Japanese troops attacking Peiping and Tientsin. Is it a withdrawal, an attack, a truce, or a fierce battle? This contradictory news is truly bewildering. However, in our opinion, even if the Japanese side withdraws its troops, it is by no means without a reason, and it does not mean that it will stop its ambitions of aggression. We must vow to exert our utmost efforts to fight them to the death, but it is unexpected that so-called scholars and celebrities are criticizing the loyal and brave soldiers who are (taking off their shirts and wielding the big knives forged in the blacksmith's shop) (using flesh and blood to fight against the most cruel and modern weapons) as being contrary to modern civilization, or even saying that they are overestimating their abilities, and therefore advocating waiting for fifty years. We truly cannot understand this kind of view.

Moreover, since the abandonment of Rehe, Peiping has been under the enemy's overlooking gaze, and the people are in a state of constant anxiety. The situation in North China is also extremely complex, and crises are lurking. Even if the Japanese side withdraws its troops, it is only to lure our side into compromise in order to take a temporary rest and wait for an opportunity to advance again. If we are fooled by them and do not make the final determination to resist, then the result will be that even if we can enjoy temporary peace today, the crisis will eventually be unimaginable. If we say that today's Washington conference, where the great powers of Britain, France, and the United States are all eager to seek to stabilize the world's finances, and that in order to stabilize the world's finances, it is necessary to first restore peace in the Far East, and that Japan will inevitably take some action, and that our country still has a glimmer of hope, this kind of mentality is no different from the previous reliance on the League of Nations. What will the effect ultimately be?

As for our people, during the January 28th Incident, donations were extremely enthusiastic, and whatever was needed at the front, the rear would immediately provide. This time, the battle line along the Great Wall is 1,800 miles long, ten times longer than the battle line in Shanghai, and the spring cold is biting, the ash and sand are blowing in the face, and the mountain roads are rugged, making marching extremely difficult. The hardship is several times greater than the Shanghai battle. However, our people's donations are less than one-tenth of what they were during the Shanghai battle. This is truly something we cannot understand. Alas, the orioles are flying, the swallows are dancing, and the variegated flowers are blooming. The spring scenery in the south of the Yangtze River is indeed beautiful, and the wind is clear and the sun is bright. Our people can indeed enjoy themselves and forget their worries. However, the loyal and brave soldiers at the front are enduring hunger and cold, risking their lives, and fighting with their flesh and blood to protect the survival of our nation. Can we not feel a pang of conscience when we reflect on ourselves? Moreover, can we continue to watch from the sidelines for long? In short, today, the matter has become urgent. Should we fight or not? Our government and people must think about it thoroughly.

Song Ziwen to Go to US to Urge Countries to Pay Attention to Sino-Japanese Case, Restore World Economic Prosperity

Plan to Take Advantage of Washington Talks 49

Leave Guo Taiqi in Geneva to Preside

Soviet Union Tends to Support Our Country's Position

(Geneva) After meeting with key figures in France and Britain in Paris and London, Chinese representative Gu Weijun returned to Geneva this morning. He stated that he will take a ship to New York on Saturday to confer with Finance Minister Song Ziwen and US officials on various issues. Gu believes that if the Far East is not stabilized, efforts to restore world trade and large-scale disarmament will be futile. Therefore, this trip will ask the US government to take swift and decisive action on the Manchurian issue. It is reported that after Gu arrives in the US, he will first report to Song Ziwen on his recent talks with key European figures, and then the two will meet with US President Roosevelt and Secretary of State Hull to discuss everything. Since Roosevelt and British Prime Minister MacDonald will discuss disarmament and general peace, as well as the world economic situation, Gu plans to take the opportunity to strongly emphasize the importance of resolving the Manchurian issue for restoring the world economy, so as to avoid further bloodshed in North China, and to make an agreement on disarmament possible. Moreover, according to Gu's opinion, if military activities in North China are not stopped, China and Japan will have to sever diplomatic relations. As for the Soviet Union's attitude, diplomatic circles here generally believe that it agrees in principle with China's view that economic recovery can only be achieved after world peace. Therefore, the Soviet Union will support China's position at the London Economic Conference in the future. (National Telegram on the 25th)

League of Nations Studies Non-Recognition of Puppet Organizations from a Legal Standpoint 50

Secretariat Drafts Report for Submission to Advisory Committee

Wait for Results of Washington Talks Before Taking Concrete Action

(Geneva) The League of Nations Secretariat has completed its legal study of the policy of non-recognition of puppet organizations and has drafted a report. It may be sent to the advisory committee members at the end of this week, and it is expected that a full meeting of the advisory committee will be convened thereafter. There is an impression here that the major powers are not eager to implement an arms embargo, preferring to intensify world public opinion against the non-recognition of puppet organizations. League of Nations members and other diplomats are closely watching the talks in Washington to see if the Far East issue will be raised. It is generally believed that the League of Nations members will not be able to take any concrete action against Japan and Manchuria until they see the results of the Washington talks. (National Telegram on the 25th)

Russian Officials Deny Sino-Russian Non-Aggression Pact 51

(Moscow) TASS News Agency, citing official sources, formally denied the news reported by the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun and the Japanese Telegraph Agency that the Soviet Union had begun negotiations with the Chinese government on a non-aggression pact. (TASS Telegram on the 26th)

New Progress in Washington Talks

US, Britain, and France Hold Trilateral Meeting 52

Prepare to Sign Consultation Treaty to Guarantee Peace and Develop Trade

Understanding Reached on War Debt Issue Between Britain and US

Opinions Converge on Adoption of Bimetallism Among Three Countries

MacDonald Leaves US Yesterday to Return Home 53

(Washington) Today, US President Roosevelt and British Prime Minister MacDonald met with several experts at the White House. Afterward, experts from France and the US gathered with Secretary of State Hull at the State Department to discuss matters. At noon, Hull hosted a banquet for MacDonald, Herriot, and Canadian Prime Minister Bennett. It is reported that Bennett's visit to the US, in addition to general talks, is also to prepare to negotiate a reciprocal trade agreement with the US for many items not included in the Ottawa Agreement. The first trilateral meeting between US President Roosevelt, MacDonald, and Herriot will be held tonight. (National Telegram on the 25th)

(Washington) US Secretary of State Hull has given a strong indication today that Britain, the US, and France now believe that a guarantee of peace is a necessary condition for the world's economic recovery. Hull stated that the US is willing to sign a consultation treaty with other countries under certain limitations, and indicated that signing this treaty would encourage international trade. However, while the US is willing to sign this treaty, it does not want to bear the actual responsibility of intervening. According to the State Department's disclosure today, this attitude is sufficient to confirm the previous rumors that talks between the US President, the British Prime Minister, and the former French Prime Minister discussed the issue of restoring international trust. (National Telegram on the 25th)

(Washington) French representative Herriot and Canadian Prime Minister Bennett have now arrived here, and the scope of the talks is expanding. This morning, the delegations from the US, Britain, France, and Canada each met separately with their experts to discuss everything. Tonight, Britain and the US will hold their final meeting. British Prime Minister MacDonald is scheduled to return to London tomorrow, but the British experts who came to the US with the Prime Minister will remain in Washington to complete the few remaining items. German Central Bank President Schacht will arrive here with experts on May 5. (Reuters Telegram on the 25th)

Understanding Reached on War Debt Issue Between Britain and US 54

(Washington) According to an official announcement released this afternoon, President Wisforth and British Prime Minister MacDonald discussed the war debt issue today, and both sides have reached a clear understanding of the issues involving Britain and the US. Although a solution has not yet been decided, there has been good progress, and these negotiations will continue in Washington and London in the future. (Reuters Telegram on the 25th)

(Washington) Progress has been made on a satisfactory solution to the war debt issue and efforts will continue in London and Washington after MacDonald leaves the US. This statement was released in a joint communiqué issued tonight by Roosevelt and MacDonald, who held a trilateral meeting with Herriot tonight before suddenly summoning the Senate Foreign Relations Committee to the White House at about 10 p.m. The communiqué was issued after the Foreign Relations Committee went to the White House to consult on opinions. The attitude of the senators was not disclosed in the communiqué, but it is expected that they generally agree with the understanding reached by the three leaders thus far. However, this understanding should not be regarded as an agreement to amend the war debt structure. It only means that the US President and the British Prime Minister have found a possible path to a solution. The fact that the communiqué was signed only by Roosevelt and MacDonald is because Herriot did not participate in all the talks. However, Herriot stated when meeting with reporters that he fully agreed with what has been discussed at the White House so far, which can also reveal his attitude. The US President's sudden summons of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee to the White House is expected to consult on the opinions of the Senate on the war debt issue and some economic proposals. It is reported that a certain proposed solution was presented to the senators, and several expressed their support. However, former Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee Borah did not go to the White House and did not state the reason for his absence. Although it is now believed that Borah must have been invited beforehand and asked to explain the reason for his absence, as there is no excuse to refuse the White House's summons, it is estimated that a new precedent will be set in official etiquette. Borah's usual attitude is to advocate exchanging special trade rights for war debts. (National Telegram on the 25th)

Opinions Converge on Adoption of Bimetallism Among Three Countries 55

(Washington) It is heard that the issues considered by the US authorities and the British and French representatives include bimetallism, so as to use more silver as a monetary base. It is rumored that the US proposed a plan to reduce the US currency's gold reserve from 40% to 35% and to supplement the reduced 5% with silver. However, this plan may not be implemented unless it is agreed to by other countries. (Reuters Telegram on the 25th)

(Washington) The talks between the British and US representatives ended here tonight. The progress made has exceeded the expectations of both sides before the British Prime Minister arrived in Washington. It is heard that a general basis of understanding has been established, and a solid basis for consolidating the currency system is also included. It is heard that the talks between the French and US representatives are the same as those between the British and US representatives, and they also discussed adopting a bimetallic system and reducing the gold reserve by a certain percentage and replacing it with silver. (Reuters Telegram on the 25th)

(New York) The New York Tribune's Washington dispatch stated that, according to appearances, if the US wants to lower the value of the US dollar, the Canadian authorities are prepared to follow the US's monetary behavior and are prepared to support the US experts' informal proposal to include a certain percentage of silver in the central bank's gold reserve. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

British Budget Does Not Include Repayment of US Debt, US Officials Do Not Find It Strange 56

(Washington) The British budget does not include the provision to repay the debt owed to the US on June 15. This move was expected by the Americans, as the previous year's budget also did not have this provision. Although officials are paying attention to this matter, they do not attach much importance to it. France's attitude towards the debt due in June is still undecided. Some here say that Britain's open disregard for the issue of debt repayment is influenced by the Farm Relief Act of the US, the Thomas Amendment, which advocates allowing the President to allow debtor countries to repay debts with silver up to 100 million yuan. India has a large amount of silver reserves, and the method of repaying debts with silver is very convenient for Britain. (Reuters Telegram on the 25th)

Date of Opening of Economic Conference Determined 57

To Be Held in London on June 12

(Washington) President Roosevelt and British Prime Minister MacDonald have agreed that the World Economic Conference will open on June 12. This proves that the talks between Britain and the US have made progress. The World Economic Conference Organizing Committee, which is scheduled to meet in London this Saturday, will therefore definitively decide that June 12 will be the opening date of the Economic Conference. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

Inflation Plan Fervently Debated in Senate 58

(Washington) President Roosevelt's inflation plan has made progress in the Senate today, despite heated debate between Democrats and Republicans. Republicans say the move is unconstitutional and shakes the public's trust. Democrats, on the other hand, support it, saying it is a cautious plan and not unlimited inflation. Government leaders expect the bill to pass tomorrow without changes, while there are rumors that several compromise solutions are being considered, one of which aims to remove the power to reduce the gold content of the currency and replace it with the minting of more silver coins or the purchase of silver. (Reuters Telegram on the 25th)

Experts Support Reduction of Gold Content in US Currency 59

(New York) The National Committee, composed of hundreds of industry and agricultural leaders and economists and financiers who support reducing the value of US currency, claims that the committee's experts have calculated that in order to restore the purchasing power of the US dollar to its 1926 level and to raise prices to their 1926 level, the gold content of the US dollar must be reduced by 42.8%. According to experts, reducing the value of the US dollar only requires raising the price of gold to $36.17 per ounce, and the authorities should find a way to achieve this goal. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

Republicans Propose Free Minting of Silver Coins 60

(Washington) It is rumored tonight that Republicans and Democrats who advocate the use of silver are now planning to form a mixed group to eliminate the clause in the inflation bill that reduces the gold content of the US dollar and replace it with an amendment for the free minting of silver coins. The proposed ratio between gold and silver, according to unconfirmed sources, is 25 to 1. The Washington correspondent of the Wall Street Journal pointed out that the mixed action of Republicans and Democrats is a plot by those who oppose the Thomas proposal to use silver bullets to kill this bill, but it is expected that their plot will fail, and the Thomas proposal will be passed by 60 votes. From the perspective of the government-appointed senators, the reduction of the gold content of the US dollar is legal, so they will strongly resist any changes. The Thomas proposal is an amendment to the Farm Relief Act, authorizing the Treasury Department to consult with the Federal Reserve Board to purchase 300 million yuan of government bonds. If the purchase of government bonds cannot be negotiated, the President can directly issue 300 million yuan of Treasury bills. The President can also reduce the gold content of the US dollar, but not by more than 50%. The US can allow other countries to repay debts with silver, up to a value of 100 million US dollars, and the price of silver cannot exceed 50 cents per ounce. The US can issue silver certificates based on the amount of silver it receives from foreign governments. The above is the plan in the Thomas proposal. Now some people are advocating to increase the amount of silver allowed for foreign repayment of debts to 250 million yuan. (Reuters Telegram on the 25th)

Nine South American Countries Accept US Invitation 61

(Washington) Nine American Latin countries have accepted the invitation of the US government to participate in the Washington talks. Argentina, Brazil, and Mexico will all send special representatives, and the remaining countries will each send their ministers to Washington as representatives. (Havas Telegram on the 25th)

India-Japan Commercial Treaty Cancellation Incident: Japan Hopes World Economic Conference Will Resolve Boycott of Indian Cotton, Believes It Is Harmful and Useless 62

(Tokyo) The opinion in the business community is that unilateral trade is impossible. If India refuses to buy Japanese goods, then Japan will have to retaliate. Someone inquired with the Commerce Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs whether Japan would buy raw cotton from the US. The spokesperson of the bureau replied that he did not know, but everything depends on what India wants to do. The official also mentioned the commercial relations between India and Japan, saying that except for last year, they have always been beneficial to India. If the Indian government had given Japan a chance to discuss everything before implementing the strict plan to cancel the India-Japan commercial treaty, it would have greatly benefited the long-term friendship between the two countries. The Japanese business community claims that the depreciation of currency is temporary. As for trade barriers, once they are erected, they are difficult to remove. When the yen depreciated by 20%, India had already increased the import tax on Japanese goods from 30% to 50%. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

(Tokyo) Although some people in the Japanese cotton textile industry advocate that Japan should boycott Indian cotton when the London Seymoura talks fail, as a retaliatory plan for the abolition of the Japan-India commercial treaty, officials believe that this boycott is harmful and useless to Japan. This is because Japan's move will cause the price of Indian cotton to fall, allowing competitors to purchase cheaper cotton, and the raw cotton that Japan needs to purchase from other places will inevitably rise in price. Officials now have high hopes for the world economic discussions in both Washington and London, but the government seems to expect that a solution can always be established along the lines of an agreement to regulate exports. (Reuters Telegram on the 26th)

The Situation of the Restoration of Diplomatic Relations between the US and Russia 63

The US Sets the Reorganization of Old Russian Debts as a Condition

Congressional Members Tend to Recognize Russia with Increasing Force

(Washington) The restoration of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia, according to tonight's situation, is expected to be still far off. Reliable sources say that the Soviet government has yet to express its willingness to reorganize or consider the debts owed to American officials and businesses before the establishment of the Soviet government. It is said that someone informally inquired about this matter with the Soviet Union some time ago, but there has been no reply. As for the attitude of the United States, although it does not insist that the entire amount of 768,583,000 gold dollars owed to American officials and businesses during the old Russian era must be repaid in full, it strongly advocates that the Soviet Union must recognize and reorganize this debt to avoid setting an unprecedented historical precedent. It is also heard that the US State Department anticipates that the Soviet Union will propose a counter-proposal after the start of negotiations,

demanding compensation for losses and damages caused by the US military's intervention in Siberia. It also anticipates that the Soviet Union will propose repayment over a long period after recognition, and pay it together with the interest on new debts borrowed thereafter. The US government also has answers to this, but Russia has so far made no indication of recognizing the old debts. At present, the forces in the US Congress who support recognizing the Soviet Union are quite strong, and there is hope that diplomatic relations can be restored before the London Conference. The government is also willing to handle it in the manner of the restoration of diplomatic relations between Britain and Russia in 1924. As for the issue of communist propaganda after recognition, the US government is not afraid, and it is expected that mutual agreements can adequately prevent mutual interference in internal affairs. Moreover, the Communist Party only had 102,000 votes in the last presidential election in the United States, indicating that its power is gradually declining. (National Telegram, 25th)

Matsuoka Quietly Returns to the Country 64

Plans to First Return Home to Comfort His Elderly Mother

Declines All Formal Welcomes

(Tokyo) Matsuoka Yosuke and his party will

arrive in Yokohama on the afternoon of the 27th and immediately take a special train to Tokyo. Secretary Kishi, specially appointed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, served as the welcoming preparation committee and prepared various welcoming items. After that, he telegraphed Matsuoka on the ship to inquire about the time, etc. However, Matsuoka replied that he was very grateful for the welcome from all parties, but after arriving in Japan, he planned to return to his hometown to comfort his elderly mother, so he declined all formal welcomes. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, respecting Matsuoka's opinion, cancelled unnecessary welcoming preparations. At that time, the Foreign Minister and key figures from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will personally welcome him at Tokyo Station. (Japanese Allied Telegram, 26th)

Disarmament Conference Reopens British Plan Suffers a Major Blow 97

China, France, Russia, and Six Other Countries Submit Amendments

US Representative Emphasizes Policy of Mutual Consultation

Gu Weijun Declares Prevention of Militarism 98

▲Reuters Geneva Telegram, 25th: The General Commission of the Disarmament Conference reconvened today. China, Turkey, France, Russia, Poland, and Norway all submitted amendments to the British draft. Dr. Gu Weijun, the Chinese representative, explained the purpose of the Chinese amendments, saying that the effect of these amendments is to strengthen the restrictions on the use of force. Therefore, the numbers (using war or force to resolve international disputes) have been revised in order to prevent various armed acts that endanger world peace and the safety of the people. Other points of the Chinese amendments are aimed at the early conclusion of the Disarmament Convention and making it effective so as not to undermine existing peace tools. Dr. Gu also proposed a clause as follows: (The signatory countries, which are also members of the League of Nations, hereby declare that the existing form of the convention shall not prejudice the rights and obligations of the members of the League of Nations, nor shall it conflict with the powers of the Executive Council under the League of Nations Covenant). After the other five countries successively stated the scope of their amendments, the General Commission adjourned until tomorrow. The British disarmament plan was submitted to the General Commission last month, suggesting numerical limits for European troops and quantitative limits for tanks and mobile heavy artillery. It also suggested that the Maritime Disarmament Convention should be popularized as far as possible. All aerial bombardments, with a few exceptions, should be prohibited. The British disarmament plan also mentioned chemical, bacteriological, and incendiary warfare, naval and air aircraft, and advocated that Germany should be exempt from the naval restrictions in the Treaty of Versailles, but its existing status should continue until the end of 1936.

▲Havas Geneva Telegram, 25th: The General Commission of the Disarmament Conference was able to start its work. The French delegation specifically published a document on a part of the British proposal related to the security issue, stating that France advocates submitting the issue of consultation treaties to the General Commission. France will express its opinions on this matter after waiting for countries outside the League of Nations to explain their views. The Political Committee had previously decided to organize a sub-committee to draft the European Mutual Assistance Treaty. France intends to submit a complete proposal on the issue of local treaties after this sub-committee is organized. However, France intends to propose the following claims immediately, namely (1) Publish a declaration of non-use of violence to bind all European countries, (2) Conclude a general treaty to promote methods of preventing war, (3) The following two types of countries have the right to enjoy assistance, (A) Countries participating in the general treaty, when encountering various situations stipulated in existing security treaties or security treaties that are about to be signed, (B) European countries, when subjected to obvious violations. What constitutes obvious infringement should be determined within the European scope according to the suggestion of the Soviet Union, (4) Establish supervisory committees in the capitals of various countries, (5) The mutual assistance measures agreed upon by European countries shall be implemented, (6) Conclude a financial mutual assistance treaty, all European countries shall be bound.

▲Havas Geneva Telegram, 25th: The General Commission of the Disarmament Conference reconvened. Chairman Henderson and US Representative Davis, on behalf of his colleagues, congratulated Mr. Henderson on his new Carnegie Endowment for International Peace Prize. The committee immediately discussed the part of the British proposal related to security issues.

The Polish representative proposed three amendments: (1) Argued that the League of Nations Covenant and the Paris Non-Aggression Pact should be included in the future disarmament convention as part of the convention, (2) Argued that the obligations stipulated in the British proposal regarding (prohibiting engagement in war) should be extended to (prohibiting the use of violence), (3) The signatory countries of the future disarmament convention, whether or not they are members of the League of Nations, may initiate the convening of consultation meetings in accordance with a procedure in the event of an incident. This procedure will be determined separately. The Polish representative specifically requested the United States to participate in the consultation treaty.

▲Reuters Geneva Telegram, 26th: When the General Commission of the Disarmament Conference met this afternoon, US representative Davis announced the US's attitude towards security issues, saying that although the US supports (the policy of mutual consultation), the provisions of the British draft regarding mutual consultation are too strict. The United States will announce its acceptable methods of mutual consultation later, but this method is tied to the degree of disarmament achieved and is especially related to the reduction of aggressive armaments. After a general discussion, it was felt that the British plan was not well received, so it was decided not to put it to a vote. The General Commission then adjourned. The meeting was very short, and it will reconvene tomorrow.

Shiba Products Japanese Pearl Merchants Daydream 99

▲Japanese Allied Telegram, 26th, Tokyo: Mikimoto Shoten, Japan's largest pearl merchant, is producing a model of the residence of the first US President Washington with pearls for the Chicago World's Fair. It is scheduled to be shipped to the United States on the Heian Maru on May 2. The model is 1.6 feet long and 8 inches wide, using a total of 24,000 pearls, worth 620,000 yuan at current prices.

Final Estimate of British Financial Prospects Surplus of Over One Million Pounds 100

▲Reuters London Telegram, 25th: Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain said in his budget speech that the beer tax would be reduced, but retail prices must also be reduced, and the wine trade must be improved. Therefore, the beer tax will be completely changed so that those who improve the quality can reduce the price by one penny per item. It is estimated that the reduction in the beer tax will reduce government revenue by 14 million pounds. He also said that there is absolutely no reason to be pessimistic about Britain's financial prospects. If guided by sound and experienced principles and policies, there will be no danger to Britain's finances. Income tax cannot be reduced at present. The payment of income tax has always been divided into two times a year. In the previous term, three-quarters of the total annual income tax had to be paid at the first payment. Now, this method is inconvenient and it is still changed to be paid in two equal installments. Other than that, there are no other changes. Chamberlain announced that the final estimated income was 698,777,000 pounds and the expenditure was 697,486,000 pounds. The estimated surplus was 1,291,000 pounds. The Chancellor's speech lasted two hours and seven minutes before it was finished.

▲London Telegram, 26th: Chamberlain's second budget after taking office as Chancellor of the Exchequer was stable and without brilliance. Even those who support the government are not very interested in it. The Times pointed out that the Chancellor of the Exchequer lacked imagination. It is generally believed that the stability of the financial situation and the shrinkage of tax sources should be a reason for making extra efforts to help trade recover. The only thing that can be noted is that the changes in tax rates in the budget are political rather than financial in nature. The increase in the tax on heavy oil is to protect the coal industry, and the new tax on motor vehicles is to help poorly performing railways, while the reduction in beer tax is to encourage breweries to use more domestic buckwheat.

Britain Implements a Ban on the Import of Russian Goods 101

▲Reuters London Telegram, 25th: The House of Commons discussed the case of the trial of British technicians from the Vickers Company in Moscow today. Foreign Secretary Simon replied to questions, saying that after the four technicians returned to London, they reported the course of events to the Foreign Office and insisted that Thornton and McDonnell were completely innocent, as were they. Now they are still imprisoned and have not been released. Simon continued, "I have personally seen four people (the crowd cheered). I firmly believe that the accusations against them are deliberately fabricated. The British government's actions regarding the entire case are completely justified." The British ban on the import of Russian goods will be implemented after the customs close at 5:00 pm tonight. Goods that arrive after tonight will not be allowed to be declared and must be shipped back to Russia or to other countries.

A Net to Catch Airplanes in the Sky 102

▲French Invention of an Anti-Aircraft Weapon

▲Reuters Marseille Dispatch: France has recently invented a powerful anti-aircraft weapon, which is a fine net of pure steel, suspended in the sky by balloons, about two and a half miles from the ground, to catch attacking enemy aircraft. The wonderful thing is that the enemy aircraft cannot see this net. It is currently being tested in Toulon.

Czech Foreign Policy Advocates Maintaining the Status Quo 103

Will Conclude a Treaty of Friendship with Poland

▲Havas Prague Telegram, 25th: Foreign Minister Benes said in a speech to Parliament that when Germany and Italy adopt a policy of amending treaties, the Czech Republic has two purposes. First, small countries being sacrificed to the mutual jealousy of strong countries is a thing of the past. The Czech Republic will do its best to prevent it from being seen today. Second, the coordination of various small countries will ensure that the governments of European countries are still based on democracy and oppose modifying the procedures of the League of Nations by arbitrary methods, and part of the affairs under the jurisdiction of the League of Nations will be removed and not allowed to be handled. Benes mentioned the amendment of treaties, saying that no independent country can allow other countries to use political and spiritual power to arbitrarily decide on its territory, or mutually compromise. Benes recalled that when he was previously in Geneva, he had told British Foreign Secretary Simon that he could not force certain countries to correct their borders. He said at the time, "If anyone plots against the Czech Republic, no matter what he plots, this person must come armed to seek the land he covets." Benes also said that even if the clauses on land in the treaty do need to be amended, it must be done after a long period of preparation, with fair compensation, and after direct compromise and free recognition by the countries concerned. The Foreign Minister believes that there is only one way to seek sound and fair cooperation among countries, that is, all countries, regardless of size, should compromise directly and frankly and exchange views with each other. As Benes's speech was coming to an end, he announced that the Czech Republic hopes to sign a treaty of friendship with Poland soon.

Our Swastika Society Provides Relief to California Earthquake 104

▲Reuters Washington Telegram, 26th: The Washington Red Cross has received 100,000 yuan in relief funds for the California earthquake remitted by the Chinese Swastika Society.

The Course of the Xinjiang Incident

Jin Shuren's Improper Measures The Hui Rebellion Has International Backgrounds The Future of Xinjiang Province Is Extremely Dangerous 105

Beiping Correspondence: The occurrence of the Hui Rebellion in Xinjiang coincided with the urgent invasion of North China by the Japanese, which has aroused the attention of the Chinese people. Recently, a certain important person from Xinjiang living in Beiping talked about the course of the Xinjiang Incident and the recent situation in Xinjiang Province. It is described as follows for the reference of the Chinese people.

Causes of the Incident 106

Xinjiang is located in the northwest of our country, spanning thousands of miles. It is a vast land with abundant resources and rich products. On the southern route of the Tianshan Mountains, there are tens of thousands of acres of fertile land and millions of residents. It is indeed an important area on the northwest border of our country. During the tenure of Yang Zengxin as the governor of Xinjiang Province, the old system was maintained, and the government and the people were able to live in peace. The current authorities are oppressing them very urgently, and the people are becoming more and more alienated. The people of Xinjiang Province are mostly Hui people, and they are strong and united. The feelings between the two sides are getting worse day by day, leading to the rebellion.

Loss of Hami 107

The region of Hami is a crucial town in the eastern part of Xinjiang. During the late Qing Dynasty, it had a Hui King (Muslim King) overseeing its governance. After the establishment of the Republic of China, the position was still hereditary, managing the rental of its enclosed lands and trivial matters of the Hui people. The king enjoyed considerable influence due to the deep faith of the masses. When it came to the reign of Shamo Husuote (called "Prince Sha" by the Han people), his tyranny and arrogance gradually alienated the people. Last spring, when Shamo Husuote passed away, the Hui people, dissatisfied with the behavior of the young Hui King Niezi'er, sent representatives to meet with Chairman Jin Shuren, requesting that the Hui King position not be succeeded. They offered to pay all due taxes directly to the provincial government to alleviate their suffering. Jin initially agreed, but later, influenced by his subordinates, he broke his promise and confiscated all the Hui people's enclosed lands, stirring up popular resentment. At the beginning of this month, the people rose up, disarmed the provincial army stationed in Hami, and occupied the city of Hami.

Distress Call from Dihua 108

Jin Shuren was originally from Didao in Gansu province. The majority of his troops were his fellow townsmen. They had a full nominal roster, ostensibly five divisions, but were understaffed, lacked training, and were extremely weak. Once an incident occurred, dealing with it would be exceedingly difficult. In this recent Hui rebellion in Hami, the Hui people's weapons were mostly supplied by a certain country and were exceptionally sophisticated. After capturing Hami, they advanced westward and occupied the Gongdao Ridge in Zhenxi (west of Hami). The Hui people of Kashi, Kashgar, and other areas of the southern route of the Tianshan Mountains, as well as the Mongol people of Alxa, rose up in response. It is rumored that Ma Zhongying's troops, stationed in Gansu, have also departed from Jiayuguan (the end point of the Great Wall and a strategic point for transportation between Gansu and Xinjiang) and are advancing towards Hami. Their intentions are yet to be confirmed. Currently, Dihua (Urumqi, a major town in the northwest) is in extreme danger. If the central government does not swiftly devise a good plan, the situation may escalate.

Soviet Russian Aggression 109

Xinjiang has a vast territory and abundant resources, long coveted by the great powers. After Outer Mongolia's defection, Russia focused nearly all its efforts on Xinjiang, first with economic aggression and then with cultural offensives. Other countries such as Turkey, England, and Japan also had plans. When Yang Zengxin was in power, he traded with Russia but strictly prohibited direct transactions between merchants and citizens. All imported goods were handled by the government, which then distributed them to merchants and citizens. The price levels and import quantities were strictly limited, causing great distress to Russia. Now, these restrictions are gradually being relaxed, and foreign goods flood the new province, with low prices. Domestic goods are almost ignored. The loss of economic rights is imminent, and the future is dire. As for the province's education, it is extremely rudimentary. Newspapers are mostly run by Russians. Thinking of this, one cannot help but feel a chill.

Japanese Scheme of Intervention 110

The various forms of Soviet Russian aggression are already alarming, but Japan is even more ambitious and aims to intervene. Although its distance makes economic aggression difficult to advance, its intentions are far-reaching, and it has many sinister schemes. In addition to establishing various newspapers in the new province as propaganda tools, it also actively connects with the Hui people to expand its influence in the new province. Recently, it has built a large-scale mosque in Tokyo, granting Japanese people permission to worship Islam to show goodwill. Currently, there are over 250 Hui students studying in Japan. The expansion of Japanese influence in the new province should not be ignored. Furthermore, the Hui people have developed a great aversion to the Russian coercion in Tashkent regarding pig farming, creating a favorable opportunity for the Japanese to advance. The international backdrop of this Hui rebellion is extremely prominent. It is hoped that our government authorities will quickly devise a good rescue plan to prevent a repeat of the Outer Mongolia and Northeast incidents and prevent our great land from falling under the iron hooves of foreign races.

Bai Zili's Conversation 111

According to Bai Zili (Chief of the Confidential Section of the Newly Compiled Thirty-sixth Division), representative of Ma Zhongying, Ma Zhongying's division has indeed sent troops out of Jiayuguan and stationed them in Anxi, Dunhuang, Yumen, and other counties. It is unclear whether this is to guard against the Hami unrest or to join the Hui-Mongol army in Hami to confront Jin Shuren. However, I received a telegram from Ma Zhongying on the 19th, which did not mention this matter, and it confirmed that Ma himself was still in Suzhou within Jiayuguan and had not left the pass. However, Chairman Ma Hongkui of Ningxia recently gifted our division with wireless telegraphs and multiple machine guns for military use (24th).

Situation After the Defeat of the Jiangxi Bandits 112

Chiang to Go North after Completing Military Arrangements

Jiangxi West and South to Be Separately Handled by Hunan and Guangdong

Jiangxi East Military Affairs to Be Completely Commanded by Liu Zhi

A telegram from Nanchang reports that after Chairman Chiang went north the other day, the communist bandits, believing they had an opportunity, came out in full force. Zhu Mao's pseudo-First Front Army, Fang Shao's pseudo-Tenth and Eleventh Armies, Li Tianzhu's pseudo-Eighth Army, Kong Hechong's pseudo-Sixth Army Corps, and various pseudo-guerrilla teams and pseudo-independent divisions, brigades, and battalions, moved towards Nanchang via the Gan River, Fu River, Xin River, attempting to invade the city. Later, Chiang rushed back to Nanchang to take command, driving the bandits out of Qingjiang, Jinxian, Linchuan, and other areas near the provincial capital. Xingan and Dongxiang were gradually recovered, and Yongfeng and Lean were relieved from siege. The bandits were thus thwarted. Currently, the pseudo-First, Third, and Fifth Army Corps of Zhu, Mao, and Peng have all retreated south. Headquarters received a telegram from Chen Cheng, stating that "the pseudo-Third Army Corps has fled from Zhaoxie Shanhe south of Lean, hoping to reach Wangxian, Nancun, and Taipingxu, with a part fleeing to Gugang, intending to attack Yihuang. The pseudo-Fifth Army Corps of Niutian (southern Lean) and Shuinan is moving west. The pseudo-Twentieth Army has fled from Liukeng to Taipingxu, and Luo Binghui's pseudo-Twenty-second Army has fled from Xingan to Tengtian in Yongfeng." As for the recent bandit situation, on the Xin River front, Fang Shao's pseudo-Tenth Army, led by Wang Ruchi, is still in the Yujiang, Wannian, and Yiyang areas, holding onto Zhoufang and Hengfeng. After retreating to Jinxi, the pseudo-Eleventh Army intends to circle around the Fujian border and flee back to Hengfeng. On the Jiangxi West front, after the Hunan Army's Chen and Wang Divisions recovered Lianhua, Yongxin, and Ninggang, Li Tianzhu's pseudo-Eighth Army, in part, fled towards the Yuan River, attempting to join up with Li Tianzhu's troops, while another part fled east, attempting to cross the Gan River and join up with Zhu Mao's troops. The Hunan Army, fearing that the bandits would flee back, has constructed fortifications in the three counties of Lian, Yong, and Ning to defend key areas. On the Jiangxi North front, Kong Hechong's pseudo-Sixth Army Corps repeatedly launched counterattacks on the old nest of Xiaoyuan, but were repelled by the Hunan Army's Peng Weiren Division. These bandits are also trending towards fleeing northeast and are being blocked and suppressed by Tan Dao and Guo Rudong's troops on the Jiangxi-Hubei border. Overall, the situation of bandit suppression is better than before. However, since Chiang's arrival in Jiangxi, the military situation in North China has become increasingly strained. All sides are eagerly awaiting Chiang's trip north. Chiang, seeing that all of Luan East has been lost and that Pingjin is in danger, is also anxiously seeking solutions. In addition to ordering the dispatch of certain units to the front lines, he is also hastily arranging the bandit suppression affairs in the southeast in order to go north. In the past week, a basic framework has been established. Abstractly speaking, the Kong and Li bandits west of the Gan River, bordering Hubei and Hunan, will be completely suppressed by He Jian, who has been appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. Liu Jianxu has been stationed in Pingxiang to command everything. In the Jiangxi South region, the upper reaches of the Gan River above Ji'an will also be suppressed by the Guangdong and Guangxi armies, and there is also a plan for Chen Jitang to take full responsibility for bandit suppression. In the Jiangxi East region, the military affairs of the Fu and Xin Rivers will be completely commanded by Liu Zhi. With the above three routes generally determined, as long as there is coordinated action, the elimination of the communist scourge can be expected soon. Chiang can then let go of the rear and go north to command the anti-Japanese military affairs (April 21).

Groundbreaking Ceremony for the Wuhu-Zhaopu Railway 113

Engineering to Be Put Out for Bids Immediately

Survey of the Huainan Railway Completed

A report from Wuhu states that Zhang Jingjiang, General Manager of the Jiangnan Railway Company, along with Manager Pang, Zhang Xiaolin's representative Ma Yingfu, Secretary Zhou Junmei, and engineers from the Construction Committee, traveled from the capital in four cars via the Nanjing-Wuhu Road this morning. At one o'clock in the afternoon, they arrived at the Nanjing-Wuhu bus station. Gao Tie, the Administrative Commissioner of Wuhu, Ma Weilong, the Battalion Commander of the Third Training Battalion, and Mei Fo'an, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, led soldiers, patrol cars, and security teams to welcome them at the station. Many committee members of the Chamber of Commerce and representatives from the education sector also attended. Upon arrival, Zhang was introduced by Hong Shuxing, the Chief Engineer of the Wuhu-Zhaopu Road from the Construction Committee, who shook hands with the welcomers one by one. They then boarded the cars and rested at Puren Hospital. According to Zhang's speech, the Wuhu-Zhaopu Railway is very important to the transportation between Zhejiang and Anhui. It has been decided that the groundbreaking ceremony will be held tomorrow (25th) at 3 PM at the Wuhu Railway Wharf, after which bids will be solicited. Construction will begin soon. It is expected that the section from Wuhu to Sunjiapu can be opened to traffic within ten months, barring any other problems. Seventy passenger and freight cars have already been prepared. It is said that after the groundbreaking ceremony, Zhang will personally inspect the Xuanzhou-Sunjiapu route and then return to Nanjing via Wuhu. Liu Yiwu, Director of the Anhui Construction Department, also rushed to participate in the groundbreaking ceremony. It is also reported that the Huainan Railway, founded by the Jiangnan Railway Company, has now completed its survey and is also preparing to begin construction. The route starts from Bengbu, connects to the Jinpu Railway, passes through Zhengyang along the Bengbu-Hefei Highway to Hefei, and then follows the Hefei-Chaoxian Highway to the Erba Town opposite the Jiang River in Wubu. It will then connect with the Wuhu-Zhaopu Road via ferry. In the future, when all the roads are completed, the rural economy will benefit greatly (April 24).

Songjiang 114

Inspection of Defense Corps in Each District

The training of the county defense corps is nearing completion. The training results of the members in each district need to be assessed, and uniforms will continue to be distributed. Wu Changding, Director of the County Defense Committee, will go to the Fourth District tomorrow, while instructors Jiang Shiyi will go to the Third District, and Wu Zongjun will go to the Fifth District, to inspect and provide instructions on how to advance.

Suzhou 115

Deserter Opens Fire and Injures People While Resisting Arrest

Yesterday (26th) morning at 8 AM, two stray soldiers appeared in Wangting Dongqiao Township. When the Fourth District Defense Corps went to arrest them, the soldiers opened fire, injuring an old woman. They then fled with their weapons towards Wuxi.

Jiang Hong's Appeal in Fraud Case Pronounced 116

Jiang Hong, the former Director of the Jiangyin Relief Home, was accused by Ji Shashi of fraud. Jiang Hong filed a second appeal, and the Higher Court sent the case to the Wuxian District Court for retrial. The verdict was pronounced yesterday (26th), overturning the original verdict and fining Jiang Hong one hundred yuan.

River and Land Police Rescue Two Kidnap Victims 117

Huangpu Town in Suzhou was looted by bandits last month, and two people were kidnapped: Xu Yunfan, the owner of a southern goods store, and Sun Xu, the wife of an iron shop owner. At that time, all the shops in the town closed. After persuasion by the District Office, the shops reopened as usual. Subsequently, the river and land police set out to search and suppress the bandits and rescue the kidnap victims. On the 25th, they rescued Xu Yunfan and Sun Xu in the southern Taihu area and seized a bandit boat.

Wuxi 118

Slight Turnaround in Silk Market Sales

This month, the silk market in this county has been sluggish due to the suspension of foreign firms and the wait-and-see attitude of users. After the United States abolished the gold standard last week, silver prices soared, and Europe and the United States started purchasing actively. Prices suddenly rose by fifty to sixty taels. Foreign firms like Zhenyi Silk Factory and Jinshuangying saw prices of up to six hundred taels. American firms opened at five hundred and sixty taels for eighty-three points of Ivannas. The benchmark silk price on the Japanese Raw Silk Exchange was 850 yen per dan. Therefore, about five hundred dan were traded last week. The price of user silk also rose with the foreign silk market, and trading was not dull.

Changzhou 119

Incest Case Occurs in Lanling Township

Zhong Pin of Lanling Township in the Sixteenth District of Wuyi, has usually been disobedient to his birth mother. The other day, he flogged his mother and injured her. Later, Zhong and his wife took advantage of the rain and the unpreparedness of the villagers to push his mother into a ditch next to the village. Villagers heard her cries for help and used long poles to pull her out of the ditch, but she was already barely breathing. It took a long time for her to recover. Madam Xu, who is already in her sixties, could no longer bear it and filed a complaint with the court yesterday, accusing her unfilial son of attempted murder. After examining the wounds and clarifying the situation, the unfilial son will be arrested and interrogated within days.

Zhenjiang 120

County Magistrate Concurrently Serves as Land Bureau Chief

The Jiangsu Provincial Land Bureau, in order to facilitate land consolidation and improve facilities, previously ordered the county magistrates of Taicang, Danyang, Wujin, Nantong, Rugao, Nanhui, Songjiang, Jiading, Shanghai, Peixian, Wujiang, Wuxi, Changshu, and other counties to concurrently serve as preparatory members of the County Land Bureau. Now that the county magistrates of the counties have been ordered to transfer their positions, replacements must be appointed in order to take responsibility. Therefore, the newly appointed county magistrates of the counties have been appointed to concurrently serve in the positions, in order to continue operations and facilitate progress.

Changshu 121

Dispute Arises over Adding Scheduled Ships

The existing routes between the county and Suzhou are served by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Jardine Matheson & Co. Ltd., with scheduled ships departing in the morning and evening. In the past year, additional mid-day and Huimin Bureau ships have been added, providing great convenience for travelers. Recently, someone has applied to the Construction Department to add early morning ships, departing at 6:30 AM from both locations. Preparations are already in place, and the ships will begin service soon. However, the original China Merchants Steam Navigation Company believes that adding an early morning ship will cause scheduling conflicts and lead to accidents due to competition. Therefore, the manager of the company has applied to the Construction Department to stop the addition of the ships. At the same time, a man named Hu Hezhou has also made a similar application. The Construction Department has submitted the applications to the provincial government, which has instructed the county to investigate and verify.

Letter Received 122

Dear Editor, the news report that an employee of the Kailuan Mining Company had a dispute with a Japanese officer in Changli and subsequently opened fire is completely unfounded, according to a message from the General Manager in Tianjin. Please correct this. Sincerely, Manager of the Kailuan Mining Company, Shanghai Office.

Dear Editor, I recently read an article in your newspaper entitled "The Situation in Xinjiang is Becoming Increasingly Serious," which included a statement by Shi Qingyang, a member of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, regarding the Hui rebellion in the new province. A correction is urgently requested. (1) There are approximately 500 naturalized Russian and Japanese residents in the new province. The provincial government has filed a report with the Ministry of the Interior. Among them, no more than 200 are technicians employed by the provincial government. Mr. Shi's statement that the new province has recruited over 3,000 White Russians and formed an army is completely unfounded. (2) Mr. Shi's statement that the provincial authorities have placed eight Hui Kings under house arrest is also untrue. Xinjiang is too far from the mainland, and the rumors are often inaccurate. Mr. Shi may have misunderstandings, and his statements are questionable. However, those who spread rumors and create trouble may exploit Mr. Shi's words, take advantage of the opportunity to create confusion, and plot to undermine the situation on the border. The fact that the Gansu-Xinjiang highway is not open to postal traffic and that mail must be forwarded via Siberia dates back to 1931, when Ma Zhongying disturbed the new province. Although he was later defeated, he still occupied Suzhou, blocking traffic. Therefore, central government agencies often entrusted our office to forward documents to Xinjiang via Russia. This has been going on for two years, not just recently. The main reason for this Hui rebellion in the new province is Ma Zhongying's agitation, with the aim of occupying the northwest and sowing discord among the ethnic groups. The two reasons cited by Mr. Shi are inconsistent with the facts. The central government has decided to appoint a senior official to inspect the Hui rebellion in Xinjiang soon. The truth will be clearly revealed. Please publish this letter to avoid misleading the public. Sincerely, Xinjiang Provincial Government Office in Beijing. April 25.

Soviet Russian Ambassador Arrived in Beijing Yesterday Morning 123

Visited Foreign Minister Luo Wengan

And Discussed the Date for Presenting Credentials

Will Return to Shanghai After Staying in Beijing for a Few Days

Soviet Russian Ambassador to China Bogomolov, accompanied by Counselor Baikoff and others from the embassy, a total of five people, took a specially prepared train car on the Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) Railway to Beijing at 9:25 yesterday morning to visit the various authorities of the National Government and to discuss the date for presenting his credentials with Foreign Minister Luo. Bogomolov will stay in Beijing for at most two or three days and then return to Shanghai. Bogomolov's wife and the manager of the Soviet Russian Far East Bank were also at the station to see him off yesterday morning. The details of Bogomolov's conversation with reporters in the train car are recorded as follows:

Specially Prepared Train Car 124

The Jinghu Railway Bureau received a telegram from Railway Minister Gu Mengyu the night before, stating that he had approved a letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stating that Soviet Russian Ambassador Bogomolov would arrive in Beijing from Shanghai on the 26th and requesting that a train car be prepared. After receiving the telegram, the bureau prepared train car number PC504 and attached it to the early morning express train on the Jinghu Railway, specifically for Bogomolov and his party to travel in.

Boarding Situation 125

Soviet Russian Ambassador Bogomolov and his party of more than ten people arrived at the North Station at 9:10 yesterday morning in two cars provided by the Soviet Embassy in Shanghai on Xinzha Road. They were then led to the platform and boarded the train car by Chief Zhao of the Foreign Affairs Office and receptionists from the Railway Bureau. This was Bogomolov's first time at the North Station.

Those Seeing Him Off 126

Those who came to see him off yesterday morning included Bogomolov's wife, the manager and his wife of the Soviet Russian Far East Bank, Russian community leaders, and Zhao Tiezhang and Zhang Mengling from the Foreign Affairs Office, as well as Chinese and Russian journalists. The Railway Bureau had specially dispatched a platoon of railway police to distribute around the station to provide protection.

Five People Traveling Together 127

In addition to Soviet Russian Ambassador to China Bogomolov, the five people traveling to Beijing yesterday included Counselor Baikoff of the embassy, Angeski, Director of the Consular Department of the embassy, Oshanin, Chinese-language Counselor, and Rover, Director of the Soviet Russian TASS News Agency. For the sake of unified publicity, Rover accompanied Bogomolov to Beijing.

Ambassador's Conversation 128

A reporter from Xin Xin News Agency also boarded the train car and met with the Soviet Russian Ambassador. Bogomolov was wearing a dark gray suit and had a pleasant smile on his face as he shook hands with the reporter. Reporter: When will you return to Shanghai from this trip to Beijing? Ambassador: This trip to Beijing is purely to visit Foreign Minister Luo and discuss the date for presenting my credentials. I will return to Shanghai in a few days and then go to Beijing again to present my credentials according to the procedure. Reporter: Will you go to Beiping (Beijing) for this trip? Ambassador: I plan to be stationed permanently in Beijing and Shanghai and will not go to Beiping for the time being. Reporter: Has a decision been made on the selection of consuls general for your country in various locations? Ambassador: The selection of consuls will be the responsibility of the Consular Department of the embassy in the future and will be officially announced after I present my credentials. Reporter: Is it true that Director Angeski of the Consular Department will also serve as Consul General in Beijing? Ambassador: Perhaps. The Consul General in Shanghai is still en route to China. Reporter: Are you planning to establish consulates in other places besides Nanjing and Shanghai? Ambassador: We plan to establish consulates in Nanjing, Shanghai, and Tianjin. As there is no immediate need for other locations such as Beiping, Hankou, and Guangzhou, it has been decided not to establish consulates there.

First Envoy 129

Since the National Government revoked recognition of the Russian Embassy in China in December 1927, relations had been in a state of change. In July 1929, war broke out over the Middle East Railway incident, and diplomatic relations between the two countries were completely severed. On December 12, 1932, diplomatic relations were restored when our representative Yan Huiqing and Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov exchanged documents in Geneva. This lasted for five years. This is the first time that a formal Soviet envoy has entered Beijing since the establishment of the National Government. Although Borodin and Galen were stationed in Guangzhou when the National Government was established in Guangdong, they were employed by the government and were not envoys.

Because They Had Not Received Notification from the Consular Body

The Matter Was Temporarily Postponed for Discussion

Municipal Government Declares It Will Not Give Up the Entire Labor Administrative Power 132

According to the Central News Agency, the Public Concession Ratepayers Meeting's passage of the amendment to Article 34 of the by-laws of the Foreign Mixed Court's Land Regulations, regarding the management of factories in the concession, is not only an overreach of authority but also a destruction of our country's sovereignty, a division of our country's laws, and a violation of international law. The Shanghai Municipal Government has declared its resolute opposition to this kind of excessive expansion of authority. The Chinese ratepayers in the Public Concession have also united to argue their case on the basis of reason. The Shanghai Municipal Council held a board meeting at 5:00 PM yesterday. Health Bureau Prevents Epidemics 144

Organizing Cholera Vaccination Teams

Scheduled to Start on May 1st

According to the Central News Agency, the Municipal Health Bureau, recognizing that epidemics such as cholera are prevalent in summer and autumn, posing a significant threat, is organizing cholera vaccination teams to protect the health of citizens and prevent infection. The program is scheduled to start on May 1st. Due to the increasing population density in the urban area, in addition to actively preparing to establish municipal hospitals, it will also take over the China Public Hospital. The details are as follows:

▲ Preparing to Establish Municipal Hospitals: The funding for municipal hospitals has long been approved by the municipal government. The location has been decided in the central area of the city, with a site of over 87 mu. Mayor Wu Tiecheng, recognizing that the establishment of municipal hospitals is a matter of urgency, has decided to allocate 400,000 yuan within the year. Therefore, the Health Bureau has drafted the hospital building styles and internal layout plans and plans to start construction in March of next year.

▲ Taking Over the Public Hospital: The China Public Hospital on Tongji Road in Zhabei was founded by Guangdong native Chen Bingqian and others and has a considerable history. It was almost completely destroyed during the Songhu War. Although efforts were made to restore it, it never regained its former glory. The bureau is eager to establish an isolation hospital in the Zhabei area to benefit the citizens. The hospital also intends to transfer it to the Municipal Health Bureau for takeover. Therefore, the Health Bureau is very willing to take it over. However, the hospital's annual expenses require about 60,000 yuan, and its income is only 10,000 yuan from the Junpu Bureau wharf donation. Therefore, the annual expenses after the takeover still need to be planned.

▲ Preventing Cholera: The bureau is organizing cholera vaccination teams to prevent cholera, advising citizens to get vaccinated to prevent disease. Its announcement states: "For the matter of announcement, cholera is a prevalent disease in summer and autumn, posing a significant threat. In order to maintain the health of citizens and prevent epidemics, we have organized cholera vaccination teams to provide vaccinations. This has been promoted for many years, and many citizens believe in it, but there are also many confused people who are unwilling to receive vaccinations. We have decided to start preventive vaccinations on May 1st and set up branches widely to achieve universality. All citizens should receive vaccinations to increase the body's resistance and protect individual health and social security. Whether individuals or groups, those who wish to be vaccinated can go directly to the branch or come to the bureau. Groups of more than 30 people can write to the bureau to request personnel for vaccination, all free of charge. Let all know."

Astronomical Telescope Shipped from Germany to Beijing 147

China has a long history of research in astronomy. The Nanjing Qintianshan Meteorological Observatory has a history of 1,500 years. Recently, the Academia Sinica has paid particular attention and will build a very large observatory on Zijin Mountain. Its main astronomical work is the relationship between world meridians, solar activity, and continental magnetism, as well as the changes in short-term constellations. The establishment of the Nanjing Observatory is the initiative of the Far East and leads all parties to cooperate with the world in research. The astronomical telescope recently purchased by the Academia Sinica from the German Zeiss factory is a reflecting telescope. The lower part of the telescope tube has a silver-plated parabolic reflector with a diameter of 24 inches and a focal length of 16 feet. The front part of the telescope tube has a small flat reflector placed at 45 degrees to the optical axis. The image of such a large mirror is reflected laterally, allowing for direct observation. Secondly, a similar convex lens can be used instead of the flat reflector, allowing the image to be emitted from the central hole to the observation point behind the large mirror, which is the lower part of the telescope tube. The focal length of the reflector system is 33 feet. Next to the large telescope tube, and parallel to it, is a smaller telescope with an 8-inch lens and a 10-foot focal length. This auxiliary mirror is still used to observe constellations when the large telescope tube is taking photographic exposures. There is also a specially made movable table and chair that uses electric machinery to move simultaneously with the celestial body. It has extremely precise machine buttons and everything else, operated entirely by electricity, accurate and ingenious, unparalleled. At the same time, it can be used by many people to observe celestial phenomena. It is the most advanced astronomical telescope in the world and the only one in the Far East, worth more than 120,000 marks. The large mirror is specially designed to capture images of celestial bodies and spectroscopic records. It has now been shipped to Beijing and can be used once the Zijin Mountain Observatory is completed. In addition to the telescope, the Academia Sinica has also widely placed many other astronomical instruments, such as an 8-inch equatorial reflector, a 6-inch astronomical camera, also manufactured by the German Zeiss factory, a 5.5-inch meridian gauge with an automatic micrometer, produced by Societe Genevoise, a 4-inch Ross camera with equatorial mount, produced by Lundin & Harvard, a spectroscopic astronomical mirror, produced by Mount Wilson, a Shortt non-pendulum clock, produced by Riefler, several low-power telescopes, and accessories, all sold by the local resident general manager of the factory, Rehe Yangxing. The picture on the right shows Minister Liu Wendao visiting the factory and taking pictures.

Five Postal Workers Pass National Examination 148

Dispatched to Various Countries for On-Site Study of Postal Services

In order to improve China's postal service, the Ministry of Communications decided to select five postal workers from across the country and dispatch them to countries such as the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, France, Italy, and Russia to study the achievements of postal services in various countries on-site, so as to serve as a basis for future reforms. Yesterday, the Postal Administration has issued orders to local post offices, requiring postal workers above the second grade and fourth class to participate in the examination. The test questions will be sent by the Postal Administration to local post offices. It is reported that postal workers participating in the examination must be proficient in at least two languages. Postal workers selected by local post offices still need to gather in Shanghai for a retest, which will be handled by the Shanghai Postal Administration. The most outstanding will be selected, and then sent to Beijing for an oral examination by personnel dispatched by the Ministry of Communications. As a result, only five people were selected. They will first inspect the various departments of the Postal Administration for 40 days, so that they can first understand the current situation of domestic postal services. After the inspection, they will take a ship and go abroad to study in various countries, and are scheduled to return to China after six months. Currently, local post offices that have received the Postal Administration's order have begun preparing for the examination.

The Taxpayers' Association Asks the Public Works Department to Correct the Overestimation of Rent and Collect Donations 154

The Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Public Concession, based on a letter from the Gongping Accountants and Lawyers Office, requested the Public Works Department to correct the overestimation of rent, which led to the donation rate exceeding the original amount, and requested that it not be paid in order to protect legal benefits. The original letter is recorded as follows:

Letter to the Public Works Department 155

"(Respected Sirs, According to a letter from the Gongping Accountants and Lawyers Office on the seventh floor of No. 6 Sichuan Road, the concession housing donation is collected at 14% of the rent. Our office has also handled it in the same way for many years, and we have been at peace with each other. However, we recently received a donation ticket from the Donation Office, which has arbitrarily increased it from 58 taels and 2 qian to 63 taels, 5 qian, and 6 fen. It is reported that the housing donation of the neighboring house has also increased at the same time. Such arbitrary estimation and addition, without any standard, is very unfair. We should ask your association to strongly negotiate and order to maintain the status quo to protect the rights of citizens. The donation of municipal revenue should be based on the actual rent as the standard. No matter what, in law and in fact, there is no room for change. Otherwise, although it is proclaimed to the public that donations will not be increased, the budget is passed, and taxes are not increased, the actual increase in donations is increasing day by day, becoming a kind of insincere and unexplained behavior. The rent for the office is 1,644 taels and 1 qian and 4 fen per year, including the water and wharfage fee. However, last year's donation ticket was counted as 1,672 taels and 1 qian. Even if the water and wharfage fee is not removed, it is 27 taels and 8 qian and 6 fen higher than the actual rent. The taxpayer has already borne 3 taels and 9 qian more than the obligation outside the law throughout the year. This year, it is 171 taels and 8 qian and 6 fen higher than the actual rent, and he wants to bear 24 taels and 6 qian of non-obligatory expenses every year. According to the donation rate, it is not 14%, but more than 15%. According to the letter, we should send a letter to your bureau asking you to correct it as soon as possible. This is to the General Office of the Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department."

Reply to the Office 156

"(Respected Sirs, I have received your letter of April 21 regarding the Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department's assessment of rent and collection of donations, which I have fully understood. The Public Works Department collects donations, and if there is an actual rent that can be used as a standard, it should be calculated based on the actual rent. Otherwise, arbitrarily estimating the rent rate, although it is still 14%, the actual increase in donations is an act of increasing donations. Your office's actual rent is 1,644 taels and 2 qian and 4 fen per year, and the water and wharfage fee must be removed. However, the bureau has already occupied 27 taels and 8 qian and 6 fen higher than the actual rent last year, causing your office to bear 3 taels and 9 qian of non-obligatory expenses. The overestimation this year is 171 taels and 8 qian and 6 fen, and you have to pay 24 taels and 6 qian more per year. The donation rate has been increased to more than 15%. You should not pay it to protect legal benefits and to protect the rule of law of the Public Works Department. We should reply to you for your reference. Gongping Accountants and Lawyers Office."

Record of the General Meeting of the Bicycle Industry in the French Concession 165

The strike by the bicycle repair industry in the French Concession against increased special donations has been mediated and compromised.
