Preliminary Notes 230

Due to the large number of participants in the 100-meter, 200-meter and 400-meter races, the preliminary rounds were held at the China Athletic Field yesterday afternoon starting at 4:30 PM. After a long period of rain, the weather cleared up and the sun shone brightly, and the spectators were very enthusiastic. A total of 24 preliminary rounds were held for the men's Group B 100-meter race, 14 preliminary rounds for the Group A and B 200-meter race, and four groups of preliminary rounds for the 400-meter race. The races continued until dusk, and all the lights were on before they were completed.

▲3,000 Spectators: After ten days of continuous spring rain, the skies finally cleared. It was generally believed that it would affect the competition. However, the heavens unexpectedly favored us, and the clouds dissipated yesterday morning, with the sun rising brightly. The lovely sunlight illuminated the vast battlefield. At around 2:00 PM, more than 3,000 people came to watch the events. Although it was not an important program, it attracted such a large crowd. It is expected that the formal opening today will be a spectacular event with a huge crowd.

▲Venue Arrangement: The China Athletic Field, which had been deserted for a long time, was given a new look yesterday. Temporary barracks for the athletes, made of reed mats, were set up on the east, north, and due north sides of the field. Each barrack had the school emblem hanging in front of the door, in various colors, fluttering in the wind, and creating a majestic atmosphere. The sides of the barracks were interspersed with scout canvas tents, complementing each other and adding to the beauty of the scene. The command platform was located on the west side of the field, built on top of the stands, and was large enough to accommodate hundreds of people to stand on the stage and look around, with a panoramic view of the entire field, which was very advantageous.

▲A Glimpse of the Results: Looking at the results of the three preliminary races yesterday, the best time for the 100-meter race was 12.0 seconds, achieved by Liu Jiaxian of Minli, while the rest were above 12.2 seconds. The best time for the 200-meter race was 25.0 seconds by Dong Yinchu of Guanghua. All the times for the 400-meter race were above 58.0 seconds. The preliminary rounds were only for qualification, and the results were not investigated in depth, or perhaps the athletes had not fully developed their skills.

▲As I Saw It: Among the athletes, Dong Yinchu of Guanghua and Guan Changfa of Nanfang Middle School, although their results were not outstanding, their body shapes were suitable, their postures were graceful, and their sprinting skills were superb, making them talents worth cultivating. It is hoped that they will perform well in the repechage and final rounds.

▲Penalty for False Starts: There were many false starts in yesterday's preliminary rounds. Each time the race started, there were always some runners who started too early, and the race had to be recalled and restarted. As a result, many runners were penalized for false starts. There were two main reasons for this: (1) Insufficient training: the athletes lacked thorough starting training during practice, so they could not start precisely when the gun fired; (2) Intentionally trying to get a head start, hoping to win by taking a chance. Both of these are not good phenomena and should be strongly discouraged.

Tidbits 231

▲Calling Out "Old Master" Three Times: Although yesterday was only a preliminary round, each school attached great importance to it as they were vying for the repechage and the finals. All the cheering squads came to the venue to cheer on their teams. The students of Minli were particularly enthusiastic. After Liu Jiayu of Minli achieved a good record in the third group of the 100-meter Group A race, the students of Minli were overjoyed. When Tang Weijun of Minli clenched his teeth and won first place in the fifth group, the students smashed through the finish line and shouted "Old Master" three times, with voices soaring into the sky.

▲River of No Return and Dog Hole: After the 400-meter race ended, the crowd, because it was getting late, headed towards the northeast edge of the field near the basketball room. There was a ditch of water about seven feet wide, with a board across it to serve as a bridge. The board was narrow and there were many people, so the crowd suffered greatly. As a result, some people who could not pass called it the "River of No Return." After crossing the River of No Return, there was a bamboo fence on the east side of the basketball room, with a small door that only allowed one person to pass through at a time, and one had to lower their head slightly. At this time, it was as crowded as chickens laying eggs. Therefore, it was also jokingly referred to as the "Dog Hole," which can be said to be both amusing and satirical.

(Note) The school names listed under the athletes' names are often difficult to interpret. The following is a summary of the main ones, with annotations as follows: (Zhizhong) refers to Zhonghua Vocational Middle School, (Model) refers to Nanyang Model Middle School, (Shangzhong) refers to Provincial Shanghai Middle School, (Private Shang) refers to Private Shanghai Middle School, (Qingzhong) refers to YMCA Middle School.

Amateur Group A Billiards

Finals of the Chinese and Portuguese Masters Day 1: Medina and Li Gongying with Very Small Difference 236

▲Medina 1,000 Points ... Li Gongying 992

The second day of the final will be held this afternoon

Chinese and Portuguese masters Li Gongying and Medina met again yesterday in the finals of the Shanghai Amateur Group A event. The two men's skills were outstanding. The battle was announced and the spectators gathered. A total of one thousand points were played in two sessions, rising and falling, and with you ahead of me and me ahead of you, the ability to change was exhausted. As a result of the competition, Medina first reached one thousand points, and Li Gongying had nine hundred and ninety-two points, with only a slight difference. Today is the second day of the final. There is only one session at 5:30 PM, with a total of five hundred points. Who comes out on top depends on the efforts of the two men today.

Threatening a Powerful Foe 237

At the start of exchanging shots, Li showed an initial burst of brilliance. Beginning with the third shot, scoring 20, 75, 5, 55, and 55, he totaled 156 points. At that time, Medina was under pressure and only scored 14 points. After several more shots, Li continued to dominate. Medina had no choice but to switch his gun and fight again, hoping to recover. By the fifteenth shot, the score was 212 to 70 in Li's favor. Medina began to improve, at one point reaching 139 to 227. Then Li scored a massive 30 and 48 consecutively, widening the gap again to 155 points.

Returning Hand-in-Hand 238

Medina's luck turned, and his shots and tactics were both excellent, just like Li's ease at the start of the game. He progressed continuously and became unstoppable. Li's golden age had faded. He resorted to a scorched-earth strategy to trap his opponent, but the enemy's momentum was strong and always successful. After 26, 60, and 24, he scored another massive 32 on the 48th shot, surpassing Li with 393 to 368. At this point, Li furiously sped up, scoring 38 in one shot, bringing them neck and neck. Soon, they both reached 499 points. It was Medina's turn, and he reached 500 points first, ending the first half.

An Eight-Point Difference 239

In the second half, Medina played strong moves first, scoring 27 and 22 in two shots, leading by 50 points. Li responded with 28 and 26 in two shots, bringing them back to a level playing field. They first saw a tie at 693, then another at 787. Medina used his amazing technique and scored a massive 83, leading again with 874 to 791. Li was unconcerned, focusing on advancing. As a result of his efforts, he was only 8 points behind, making the score 992 to 1000.

Early and Late Silkworm Seasons in Zhejiang Are Both Unfavorable 255

(Jinhua) The silkworm season in Jinhua, Jianxi, Yiwu, Fenshui and other places is the earliest. This year, farmers have failed in silkworm farming for consecutive years. Due to economic bankruptcy, they have no funds to purchase seeds. Most of them hatch native species from their own reserves. After receiving the ants, the weather was strangely cold, with continuous rain. The development of the silkworm ants was delayed, and silkworm diseases broke out frequently. The early-season silkworms were mostly damaged due to the cold rain. White muscardine and black death disease were found. All types are supplemented with late silkworms. Currently, the first batch of early silkworms has completed the third molt, and the second batch of late silkworms has also completed the first molt and have been feeding on leaves for many days. However, after the weather turned sunny and warm, there were several days of cloudy and rainy weather, coupled with sultry heat. The silkworm rooms were unusually humid and hot, and silkworm jaundice started. The transmission was very rapid. The patients' silkworm bodies showed black spots and died. Occasionally, black water was excreted and rotted to death. They died with a strange odor. Silkworm farmers felt pessimistic.

(Tongxiang) The silkworm season in the four villages is relatively late. In the past two years, farmers have suffered heavy losses due to poor harvests of silkworm cocoons. Therefore, this year's breeding parties are very disheartened. Coupled with the cold weather and slow germination of mulberry leaves, this year's silkworm season is even later, and the economy is bleak. They have no funds to purchase seeds. Now, only those who retain soil stability in Jingtang Bridge Yuxi and Gujia Port are engaged in hatching. Few people raise silkworms in Xinqiao and Tingzi Bridge. The weather was extremely cold during hatching, and thermal power was used to supplement the temperature (commonly known as fire silkworms). The collection of ants was uneven. The early gang had just started feeding after the first molt, and the late gang had just come out of the ants. The weather has been changing in recent days, sometimes sunny and sometimes rainy. The humidity is high, and the development of silkworm ants is not healthy.

Suian green tea has been picked one after another in various mountain gardens in recent days. According to a letter from Suizhuang yesterday, this year's new tea is unusually fine and tender, and the aroma is even better than in previous years. The first batch of rough tea has been weighed sporadically, and the price per load ranges from 90 yuan to 95 yuan, which is not much different from last year on average. Flour Futures Decline 260

When the market opened in the afternoon, prices for the current month suddenly declined sharply because the end of the month was approaching, and most outside buyers had to close their positions. Factories, on the other hand, were confident and remained calm. As a result, prices declined step by step, eventually falling to 2.415 yuan. Sentiment for May, June, and July was also unfavorable, while prices for August and September remained stable because factory selling was slow. However, the price of Argentinian foreign wheat continued to fall, reportedly reaching as low as 4.4 yuan. Therefore, the outlook for the long term remains uncertain. As a result, the price for the current month declined by 1.25 cents compared to the previous day. Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Guidelines for Submissions to National Products Weekly 266

This publication seeks the following types of submissions: (1) Investigations and studies on national product factories and domestically produced raw materials; (2) Discussions on improving the production and sales of national products; (3) Records of speeches and talks on the national products industry; (4) Introductions to new national product businesses; (5) Interview records of national product businesses and their leaders; (6) National product news; (7) Other interesting and valuable texts, photographs, and ?. relating to national products.

(1) Submissions are not restricted by literary style, but should be concise and vivid. Each article should be approximately 500 characters in length; articles of particular value may be up to 1,000 characters in length.

(1) Submissions must be clearly written and use modern punctuation.

(1) Authors may choose to sign their name upon publication; however, the author's real name and detailed address must be indicated at the end of the submission and sealed with a chop.

(1) The editors reserve the right to make revisions to submissions; authors who do not wish to have their work revised must state this in advance.

(1) Submissions will not be returned regardless of whether they are published; however, this does not apply to submissions with a prepaid self-addressed stamped envelope.

(1) Remuneration will be provided for submissions upon publication.

(1) Please send submissions directly to the National Products Weekly Editorial Department, Shen Bao.

National Products Weekly Advertising Rates 267

▲ Long Line: 80 characters in length, height of one line, cost of two yuan per line per insertion, minimum of 15 lines.

▲ Short Line: 40 characters in length, height of one line, cost of one yuan per line per insertion, minimum of 30 lines.

▲ This publication is published every Thursday.

National Products Forum

Two Major Obstacles to the Future of National Products 268

— Pan Yang'an

Promoting national products, using national products, everyone knows it, everyone talks about it, everyone does it. But observing the current situation, there are two major obstacles to the future of national products, which must be actively removed and resolved during this National Products Year.

(1) The Decline of the Rural Economy: The largest source of national products is the countryside, and the largest outlet for national products is also the countryside. Today, the Chinese countryside shows signs of decline everywhere, which is a major hidden worry for the future of national products. If we examine the rural areas everywhere, eight or nine out of ten farmers lack purchasing power. Although the influence of national products is gradually penetrating the interior, everyone knows that national products are inexpensive and of good quality, and everyone can say that Chinese people should use Chinese goods. But what can be done when they are as empty as a chime and have nothing but bare walls? They lack the purchasing power. Therefore, promoting national products in the National Products Year, before the most urgent problem of the decline of the rural economy is resolved, no matter how hard the publicity is, no matter how intense the work is, I am afraid that the result will be half the effort and minimal results. The immediate prerequisite is to hope that the national financial and industrial circles will take it as their responsibility to help the rural areas. How to study the improvement of seeds and planting, the improvement of agricultural tools and fertilizers, the improvement of rural life, the implementation of rural cooperation, as well as farmer loans, farmer entertainment, farmer education, farmer side business, etc., should all be done with the greatest effort and the greatest determination, wholeheartedly to help, and fully assist. If the rural economy can be resolved, then the farmers' productivity will naturally increase, and the source of raw materials will naturally feel convenient. The farmers' purchasing power will naturally be strong, and the outlet for products will naturally be large. The financial sector's circulation is flexible, and the industrial sector's business development is saving people is saving oneself, and benefiting people is benefiting oneself. This is one.

(2) The Invisible Best-Selling of Japanese Goods: Everyone knows how to boycott inferior goods, everyone can talk about it, everyone can do it, but there is no way to prevent the sale of inferior goods, no way to prevent unscrupulous merchants from selling, and no way to prevent inferior goods from penetrating the interior. Speaking of gatherings to boycott, the previous examples of anti-Japanese associations and anti-Japanese associations are chilling. Giving up eating because of choking is heart-wrenching. Try going to the market. It is clearly a Japanese product, but it is labeled as made in the United Kingdom, made in Germany, made in Italy. It is clearly a Japanese product, but it has changed its appearance, changing the sun logo to the Chinese brand. If people abandon their conscience, what can't be done? The flesh of unscrupulous merchants can be eaten, and the hearts of unscrupulous merchants can be punished. I hope that our merchants will no longer hear or ask, and let the inferior goods be like a broken bamboo, as if entering no one's land? This is the way of suicide. In the end, the future of our national products will be bleak. Therefore, today, people in the national products industry should not think that boycotting inferior goods is the government's business or society's business. They only know how to manufacture national products, only want their own business, and ignore the prevalence of inferior goods and the cunning of unscrupulous merchants. This is a big mistake. The only problem at present is to unite fair people, have a legitimate association, and make a whole counterattack, and not stop until the goal of driving out inferior goods from the Chinese market is achieved. Alas, the national disaster is deep. People often say that the government is not reliable, and the military power cannot resist it. Only economic strangulation is possible from the people. But now, even this economic resistance is impossible? What else can be said? What else can be said?

Scientific Management

The Prerequisite Steps for Implementing Scientific Management 269

— Cao Yunxiang

The purpose of implementing scientific management is to seek precision in management and increase efficiency in order to achieve greater goals. In other words, it is to make social economy progress, stable and healthy. Leaders in the industry must have the spirit of serving the society in order to guide the industry to the right path and achieve the effect of labor-capital cooperation. This mission is extremely great and cannot be achieved by using improper means to seek temporary small profits without regard to the common welfare of both labor and capital.

In the implementation plan of scientific management, there are several systems and steps that must be stipulated in advance in order to establish the foundation of the business and the foundation of management. These systems and steps are as follows:

(1) Stipulate the Organization System (Plan of Organization), from the general manager to the workers, their respective functions, powers and responsibilities, and the relationship between each other must be clearly stipulated to avoid misunderstandings and conflicts in handling affairs, and avoid the abuse of irresponsibility and evasion.

(2) Stipulate a simple notation and number (Mnemonic Classification) for a business to determine the name and save the work of copying.

(3) Stipulate a periodic reporting system (System of Reports) to enable the manager to understand the progress of the business and to have a reliable basis for improvement.

(4) Stipulate an accounting system (Accounting System) suitable for all parts of management as a tool for management. (5) Stipulate a standard activity budget system (Flexible Budgetary System), the standard must meet the standard of production, as well as the different standards of indirect consumption between the various parts.

(6) Stipulate a procurement system (Purchasing System) to meet the needs of manufacturing engineering and economy.

(7) Stipulate a market and sales analysis system (Market and Sales Analysis) to facilitate the implementation of sales plans and management systems.

(8) Stipulate a plan and management system for production improvement (Planning & Control of Product)

(9) Stipulate an engineering plan management system (Planning & Control of Engineering)

(10) Stipulate the standards of machinery (Standardization of Equipment)

(11) Stipulate a system for the receipt, storage and delivery of various materials (System for Receipt, Storage & Delivery of Materials)

(12) Stipulate the production plan and management system (Planning and Control of Production), from the order to the shipment, whether it is in stock or customized.

(13) Stipulate the mechanical repair system (Maintenance of Plant) for inspection and repair, in order to avoid the loss of temporary stagnation and the occurrence of danger.

(14) Stipulate a graded salary system (Graded Schedule of Salaries and Wages) based on the nature, importance and responsibility of the work.

(15) Stipulate an incentive bonus system (Incentive Pay), the standard must be determined by motion and time analysis.

(16) Stipulate an employee merit and demerit record system (Employee Record) to cultivate talent and promote and increase salaries.

The above-mentioned sixteen systems must be connected to each other, like the parts of a clock, closely connected, otherwise only its form will be obtained, but not its spirit, which is equivalent to being useless. Therefore, any national product factory that wants to adopt scientific management must first look at its original level of management and reorganize it to establish a foundation. However, this is not easy either. Just taking the stipulation of the above systems as an example, it will take at least several years to complete. As for a factory whose original management situation is chaotic, it is really difficult to implement scientific management suddenly in order to achieve quick results.

National Products Talk 270

Before our country opened up to maritime trade, there was no relationship between the supply and demand of goods and the West.

Management System and National Products Movement (Part 2) 271

— Gu Yuan

The people's supplies are self-produced and self-sufficient, and there is no concept of using foreign goods. We only need to look at the equipment in the old-fashioned stores to understand. The account books for collecting and paying, the inkstone, pen, ink, abacus, book clips and other supplies are all local products. However, since the reform, these old-fashioned things have been abandoned with the change of the management system. The banks can best show this phenomenon. Bank accounting is new-style bookkeeping, and because of the horizontal writing and the use of international numbers, foreign paper must be used. The cloth-bound or leather-bound covers, as well as the related fountain pens, pencils, inks, and paper, are all foreign goods. Even the abacus, a special product of our country, is replaced by a computer of foreign origin. In this way, the management system is completely new: however, abandoning national products and using foreign goods to increase trade deficits is a very serious issue. Even the newer the management system, the more Westernized the items used. Therefore, in a certain sense, the abnormal reform of the management system is a very uneconomical thing. In fact, the people concerned did not intentionally want to Westernize, but really felt that under the new management system, all supplies were more convenient to be Western-style. From this point of view, the problem still lies in our inability to manufacture equipment ourselves. Chinese people have always been casual in nature. The old-fashioned management system focused on (people). Many large-scale stores had no documents or records for all handling procedures to rely on. They were accustomed to it and did not feel inconvenient. The new management system focuses on (system); for example, each payment has a voucher, which is passed on in order, so that each person in charge can sign and be responsible. Another example is the sale of goods, from unloading to delivery, there is a document for each procedure in the middle. And the documents often have to be copied with a pencil. Domestic paper is soft and fragile, so foreign paper has to be used. In this way, the more rigorous the system, the more foreign goods are used. In recent years, the industrial and commercial circles have reformed the new management system, which cannot but be said to be an evolutionary phenomenon in the meaning of the times; however, we cannot deny that the abuse of increasing the amount of foreign goods sold is a peculiar abnormality of China.

We believe that our country's inherent management system is scattered and lax, and there is no value in preserving it. Research and improvement is the most urgent task. However, all equipment is considered to have the necessity of adopting national products as much as possible. It is best to improve the old-fashioned equipment so that it can still be applied to the new system, or to manufacture the new equipment ourselves. In this way, although the system is new, it can still adapt to the domestic environment without abuse. We hope that people who study the management system and promote national products will pay attention to it.

Don't Forget to Move Forward 273

The New Path for National Products Enterprises 274

— Jin Songtang

In recent times, the progress of national products has been rapid. It is a very optimistic phenomenon. However, if we examine why there is such a new trend, we should attribute it to the old efforts of the pioneers of the national products industry to make progress and the considerable price they paid for their hardships. Observing since last year, the national product factories have strived to unite and coordinate, and various new combinations have opened up a new life for the future of our national products. In the future, we should promote it and follow this as the goal. I will now describe it separately for my newly emerging production factories.

The establishment of the Production and Sales Cooperation Association is actually the beginning of mutual assistance between the production industry and the merchants, and it is the basic work to solve the people's livelihood problems. It is the only shortcut to strive for property construction, and the strongest weapon to prevent the invasion of imported goods. The Production and Sales Cooperation Association, which bears this important mission, has gathered domestic talents in one hall, racking their brains and worrying, studying how to block imported goods, and how to promote domestic products. On the one hand, they pay attention to improving products and strive for the progress of material forms. They concentrate their energy. Each meeting often takes half a day, but they are still tirelessly.

The Establishment of China National Products Company: The Production and Sales Association has seen that the major companies and small shops in the country all show off imported goods to attract people's attention. They all think that national products are not easy to sell and the benefits are thin. Their eyes are short-sighted and difficult to wake up, so there is an organization of a purely perfect China National Products Company. Gather the national essence in one hall to live up to the people's expectations. At the beginning of the start-up, the business has been booming, which is enough to show that the Chinese people had the heart to love the country but had no place to buy in the past. We hope that the citizens will resolutely use national products to support this emerging national product business. We also hope that the service personnel of the National Products Company will pay attention to the output of the production industry on the one hand, and also hope to take care of the needs of consumers. Therefore, the China National Products Company is indeed a valuable record in the history of the national products movement. This is the success of the first act of the Production and Sales Cooperation Association.

National Products Introduction Institute Project: The Production and Sales Association has established a considerable economic barrier in Shanghai, which is attracting worldwide attention. In order to promote its efficiency, it plans to penetrate into various places, so there are national products introduction institutes in various places, and the Shanghai General Institute is the culmination of its efforts. The task is to distribute the products to the markets in various places through introduction, investigate consumption conditions, list national product samples, and strive to make Chinese people recognize national products, distinguish national products, and purchase standards, so that producers do not have to wait for sale, and sales personnel save the trouble of selection. Merchants in various places will have such a sound organization, saving a lot of trouble, time and energy. It can be said that the mission of the Production and Sales Cooperation Association is the motive of the mobile sales team. The Production and Sales Cooperation Association has been thoughtful and has proceeded step by step in establishing national products companies in major cities and establishing national products introduction institutes in various places, and has done its best. However, over the years, we have often seen the aggressive sales methods and official propaganda policies of foreigners, which are carried out from the metropolis to the town, from the town to the village. Even the poor and remote areas have been reached, which can be said to be meticulous and far-reaching. Looking back, the Chinese people only know how to focus on the metropolis and ignore the remote areas. They sit idly by and watch the good markets in the towns and villages being occupied by foreign forces, which is one of the major reasons for the obstacles to the future of national products. Therefore, there is the motive of the mobile sales team, with hard-working personnel, hiring boats to travel around, promoting everywhere, and selling goods at will, so that the village girls can also see the truth of national products, which is a very good method.

The above-mentioned is indeed a new contribution of the China Production and Sales Cooperation Association in the past year, which is to seek the stability and progress of the national products factory business. Therefore, in order to seek progress, it depends on uniting comrades, uniting spirits, and jointly establishing a sound foundation and striving for sound facilities, in order to live up to the expectations of all parties.

Page 14

Indeed, in order to be suitable for the trend of the times.

We should work harder to consolidate and enrich the internal aspects of each individual. We also hope that the emerging factories should communicate with each other, and the people in various places should work together to benefit others and themselves. The key is to unite and concentrate. It is not difficult to reach the road to light together and get closer to the way to save the country.

The Support That the Domestic Goods Movement Should Have 275

— Ms. Bai Xue

On the surface, the domestic goods movement seems to have reached a considerably concrete and successful stage. Large factories and large domestic goods companies have sprung up one after another and are no longer uncommon. However, when we examine the reality, we still feel that it is in its infancy. For example, the tools for manufacturing domestic goods, that is, the objects for manufacturing objects—machinery—mostly rely on foreign supply. Some raw materials (like the finest yarn, rayon, etc.) are also purchased from abroad. The management systems of industry and commerce are also reluctantly imitating the superficial aspects of foreign countries. Whether they can adapt to the environment and needs of our domestic goods movement is still a question worth discussing.

The domestic goods movement should be practical and realistic and meet the needs of the nation. It should not be exclusively westernized, because this may hinder the progress of the domestic goods movement.

So, what is the support for the domestic goods movement?

(1) Scientific Support: The 20th century is an era of science. A country without science will inevitably gradually decline, leading to national subjugation. Look at our China: science is equal to zero. Large-scale enterprises (like electrical engineering, chemical engineering, manufacturing machinery, etc.) all rely on foreign countries for support. Therefore, the domestic goods movement must first cultivate great scientists to invent and create all kinds of machinery, chemical, and other large projects. In this way, the domestic goods movement can succeed, and the Chinese nation can have a country with domestic goods.

(2) Government Support: In addition to cultivating and rewarding scientists, the government should also help and build large industries. It should plan the whole country comprehensively: how to resist foreign goods? How to make the domestic goods movement a success and create a completely domestic goods-based country? How can we promote domestic goods to foreign countries? ···These are all the responsibilities of the government.

(3) Public Support: Now we are so oppressed by imperialism that we can hardly breathe, but some people still promote foreign goods and disregard domestic goods. This is a path to self-destruction. Therefore, the people should wake up and not buy foreign goods, but completely use domestic goods, so that Chinese-made domestic goods can be enjoyed by the Chinese themselves.

The above three are interrelated and cannot be separated and carried out independently. The three must advance together in unity.

Discussion of Domestic Goods

A Word for the Domestic Goods Industry 276

— Ke Ding'an

(Imitation is a bad habit of the Chinese!) Foreign friends often mock us like this. Even we Chinese ourselves often laugh at each other and gossip about it.

You should know that the word "imitation" is the most inappropriate word. As long as you are imitating, you will never succeed in anything. Because at best, it's just imitation!

The domestic goods industry in its infancy is committing the fault of "imitation." Although it cannot be said to be the majority, in my observation, it is not a small number! There is also a reason for this, which I deeply understand. Whenever a foreign product comes to China, it is popular in Shanghai, and gradually it also appears in the inland areas. When it appears in the inland areas, and it can be said that a certain foreign product is widespread, our domestic goods manufacturers then imitate that product and put it on the market. At that time, we Chinese are already accustomed to using that certain foreign product. Even if the imitation of domestic goods is as guaranteed to be similar and as solid, they will not have a need for it. Those with more discerning eyes also seem unlikely to patronize it. You should know that this is not because the Chinese do not trust Chinese goods, but because Chinese domestic goods manufacturers despise themselves too much and work as slaves for foreigners. As a result, some domestic goods manufacturers with small capital often stop halfway because the imitation of one or two foreign products does not achieve "amazing sales." This situation is not uncommon.

I believe that in order to avoid repeating the same mistakes, it is necessary to first hire specialized

talents and focus on "creation."

"Creative" products will definitely gain the approval of our Chinese people. Just look at a certain foreign product coming to China. It must be something never seen before, so curious Chinese people, you buy it, I buy it, and thus the producer of foreign goods succeeds in one fell swoop and sees great results, importing batches of them quickly, and we Chinese do not hesitate to use our great national treasures, thousands and tens of thousands, to pay tribute to foreigners.

Let's not mention anything else, let's take the XX flashlight as an example. When it first came to China, only people in Shanghai bought it for use. Now, in remote rural areas, almost ten people have one each. Although the Chinese imitate, and there is not just one producer, the sales of that foreign product are still not weaker than before, even with the imitations!

Thinking about this small example, if our Chinese producers continue to specialize in imitation and continue in this way without thinking about "creation," I think there is only the reality of regression and no possibility of progress!

Domestic goods producers who like to imitate but have no results! This is my advice. Please do not overlook it hastily. If you implement my words, eliminate imitation in the future and implement creation, and manufacture products that are extremely modern, I can guarantee that your products will definitely cater to the psychology of the Chinese people, and then you can truly achieve "amazing sales"! But don't forget these last few words!

(1) For the first product, if there are any inappropriate places, you must request the opinions of the purchasers and improve it.

(2) The product must be consistent from beginning to end, only improving and not deteriorating.

(3) If the cost of raw materials increases due to market prices, the pricing must not be deliberately raised, because it can be mutually balanced.

(4) Advertising is to assist the promotion of products and cannot be underestimated. It is necessary to hire a specialized talent to be in charge.

The Entire Economic Strategy of Domestic Goods Factories 277

— Ying

(1) Current Crisis: Chinese domestic goods factories are extremely immature. At this time of economic warfare, with short weapons meeting and blades crossing, how should our domestic goods factories carefully protect and cultivate them, so that this sprout can grow into a tall tree? Because the usual communication has not been proper enough, enemy goods take advantage of it, using their tactics of horizontal and vertical alliances, and their tricks of instigation and division, and our domestic goods factories all fall into the trap. Suspicion arises, and the trend of infighting begins, so they do not hesitate to compete in price cuts to attract customers, and indiscriminately release credit to broaden their reach. Internal war is not over, and domestic goods internal war arises again. If this continues, in a few years, people will be searching for my dried fish in the market.

(2) Relief Methods: The crisis of domestic goods is imminent. To seek relief, the first thing to do is to establish self-criticism and jointly plan for unity. However, unity does not advocate empty talk but emphasizes practicality, and does not value form but cherishes spirit. Joint sales, there have been those who have done it before, and the effect of the length is roughly visible. For the current plan, only further and most thorough unity is the best way to eliminate boundaries and unite as one family. The external business is the same for each other, the observation and listening are unified, and the atmosphere is naturally new. For each type of domestic goods factory, select a brand with better reputation and use it to achieve twice the result with half the effort. The assets of each factory are fairly estimated, and stocks are issued according to their value. The battle formation is unified, the military appearance is revitalized, the fault is removed, and clarity comes naturally.

(3) Management Strategies: The operation of industry generally values the exquisite production, especially the corresponding supply and demand, adapting to local conditions, establishing branch factories, scattered like stars, able to respond to each other, promoting the products, each near the ground, the freight is saved, and the cost is lighter. Compared to gathering in one corner, piles of old goods, land and sea transportation, often takes months, seizing the time and tending to profit, I have no ability to do it, the difference is not like heaven and earth.

(4) Profit Forecast: The united strength of the same industry is naturally powerful. When enemy goods come to invade, it is enough to fight a battle, the first benefit. The same industry united lending, at least the annual interest rate is considerable, the second benefit. Retail purchase of raw materials, the value is relatively large, since the united, you can buy in bulk at 80% discount calculation, the profit is not small, the third benefit. The same industry factories are separated from each other, the mechanical equipment, are not economical, since the united, the disadvantages are eliminated, the fourth benefit. The staff of each factory, often easy to flow, since the united, the mind is focused, and training is easy to become, the fifth benefit.

The same industry factories implement the union, the silk weaving industry, has seen the end, other factories, or more doubt, use the general description, by when the advocacy.

Domestic Goods Introduction

Nantong's Flourishing "Avenge Shame" Cloth 278

— Chen Senfu

Before introducing the "Avenge Shame" cloth, I will first describe its cause and origin: Nantong's agricultural products are mainly cotton, so the villagers mostly use weaving cloth as their only sideline. The cloth is white in color and durable in texture, so it has long been famous. Its largest market is the northeastern provinces, so the cloth shops in Tongcheng are also called "Guandong Shops." Since the September 18th Incident, when the invaders invaded and occupied the Northeast, sales plummeted. When the puppet state was established, customs duties were autonomous, and the tax rate on Tong cloth was increased by more than three times, so sales disappeared. If this continues without any consideration, wouldn't the livelihood of Nantong's weavers be completely cut off? However, the weavers did not lose heart because of this setback, but most of them automatically widened their old looms and changed to weaving plain-colored cloth with wide doorways. They were also able to carefully research and were actively promoted by various cloth shops. For a time, it became a whirlwind. After repeated discussions, today's achievements were made. The name "Avenge Shame" is taken to show the determination to avenge the national shame. The raw material for this cloth is 20-count yarn produced by the Dasheng Yarn Factory. This yarn is spun by Tonghua. The fiber length of Tonghua is 15/16 of an inch, which can spin 32-count yarn. Now Dasheng is adding a bleaching and dyeing factory, planning to dye the spun yarn into colored yarn using scientific methods, specializing in selling it for weaving "Avenge Shame" cloth, in order to make the colors bright and the quality consistent. This cloth is specified to be 7.5 zhang (old system of measurement) in length, about 5 jin and 10 liang in weight, 2.2 chi in width, and 4.67 yuan in value. It has already been sold in Jiangnan and Jiangbei and Jiahu in Zhejiang. There are also large orders in Xiamen and Shantou in Minyue. Now 1-2 thousand pi are shipped out every day. Recently, it has been heard that the wholesale goods are all sorted, packed, and shipped by the Dasheng Yarn Factory, so the wholesale office of the factory also sells wholesale. It is also heard that its Shanghai office can also place bulk orders. I wrote this article to introduce this cloth because it is purely domestic and its name is quite inspiring.

Chinese Cotton Mills Reduce Labor 279

— Zhou Chengxun

Recently, in the past week, a drastic event broke out in the local industrial community: that is, although the Chinese cotton mills have been struggling to the extreme for a year, they still could not stand firm and announced a reduction in labor. The reason for the reduction in labor is because of disastrous business failures, overproduction, and the influence of strong foreign goods dumping. They had to take this policy of controlling production to survive. For the cotton mills themselves, this reduction in labor is still a way to ease the immediate situation and slowly plan for recovery. However, this unprecedented phenomenon of absolute passivity and contradiction is ultimately a bleak page in the history of domestic industries.

People in the cotton industry say that Chinese cotton is both more expensive and of much lower quality than foreign cotton. The current state of depression is really an example of how the Chinese do not seek improvement and lag behind in everything. It is not only the cotton industry that is like this, but other industries as well. It is really useless to have the government send people to negotiate for assistance after the fact. The fundamental problem lies entirely in the self-determination and self-awareness of the producers themselves.

Implementing a reduction in labor is only a short-term transitional step and cannot cure the long-standing weakness of the cotton industry. Even throwing bombs at traitorous merchants every day cannot force them to return to their bestial nature of specializing in the sale of enemy goods for profit. If Chinese cotton can quickly put in a lot of hard work, reduce costs, and improve quality, foreign goods will lack the ability to dump, and production will definitely not be excessive. At that time, there will be too late to increase labor, where will there be a reduction in labor?

I hope that in the near future, the cotton industry can open up a new situation.

Interview

The Zhong Ting Brothers 280

— Lu Fengshi

Ten years ago, Yonghe Industrial Company was not yet of any scale. The situation was similar to the family industrial system of the Middle Ages. The entrepreneur occupied the dual position of employer and employee. It can be seen that this achievement cannot be called small.

Zhong Ting is the eldest, followed by Jiting, and then Xiangting. Perhaps they are practical people who are willing to hide their talents and do not want people to know about them. The reason why I wrote this article can be said to be

The Pyrethrum Farm of the Chinese Chemical Industry Society (Matsuzeng) 281

is based on two major viewpoints: (1) The Ye brothers have made practical contributions to the development of domestic goods. The most obvious example is the use of "Chang'e" brand toothpaste to clear away the remnants of "Diamond" toothpaste, an enemy product that was dumped across the country. (2) Among the many wealthy merchants, there are quite a few who have made their fortunes by luck, while Yonghe Industrial Company is the final crystallization of the Ye brothers' success from scratch, working day and night in rough workers' clothes.

I will also make public a story with many twists and turns, tracing back to their childhood life. From this, readers can also be sure that a difficult environment is the future opportunity, as long as you can turn resistance into assistance, then pain can be transformed into happiness.

Mr. Zhong Ting is from Qingyang Town, Jiangyin. His father was in the rice business and was also a poor man. One New Year's Day, Mr. Zhong Ting was still very young and received a small silver dollar as New Year's money. He was unwilling to spend it and quickly treasured it. After about half a year, the family suddenly hesitated over the issue of buying things, and he took out his only private savings. How could ordinary children do this?

When he first came to Shanghai to learn a trade, he was simply learning to be a nanny, washing rice, cooking, and looking after children, doing everything. He was able to endure it and did not complain at all. After three years, he was promoted to be a salesman. He was honest and responsible, so he attracted a lot of business. An elder, unwilling to bury his talents, provided him with several hundred yuan of capital and strongly advised him to start his own business. At that time, he witnessed Japanese cosmetics dominating the Chinese market, so he started a small-scale home industry, named Yonghe, which probably meant "Eternal Harmony for Generations, Sharing Great Business." However, we can also imagine that the brothers and sisters-in-law at that time were enough to encompass the two major classes of employer and employee.

Jiting graduated from the Jiangsu Third Normal School. Later, the small handicraft industry had become a small factory. He had a way to manage the economy and hoped to stand out in the cosmetics industry. He finally studied in Germany and obtained a doctorate in chemistry. The "Yongmei" cream and powder that are now sold throughout the country are the result of his many years of experimentation. Xiangting is even more shrewd and capable, simple and hardworking. If we visit their factory, we simply cannot tell that he is one of the founders of Yonghe.

I would also like to briefly describe one or two aspects of their private virtue. This is indeed the only acupuncture for modern nouveau riche. They treat their teachers with true respect. They send gifts or visit every festival, and there is no bad habit of being carried away with success. This time, when the factory caught fire, the compensation for the affected workers was also doubled compared to other factories, with thick coffins and generous funerals, caring for the workers in every possible way.

Written plainly, readers will probably have some feelings. Throughout my life, I have never wanted to write flattering words, and the main motivation for this article is entirely based on the idea of "using the facts of untouched innocence to arouse readers' interest in business."

Short Story

The Formation of Divorce 282

— Qin Shouou

Tu Zhemian was a very handsome son of a rich man, indulging in a leisurely and comfortable environment all day long. Although it was now a critical moment for the Republic of China, and everyone was worried about becoming a subjugated slave, he was still as calm as a Frenchman or an Italian who had nothing to do with the Republic of China, enjoying all the material supplies that his father had offered him to the fullest. His wife, Ms. Liu Shan, was a new woman with very noble thoughts, often donating her own money to the volunteer army and paying close attention to the war news at the front.

"I'm planning to make a new suit of clothes." One afternoon, this worthy couple, with different interests, came out of a restaurant on Nanjing Road after having snacks, and were slowly strolling along the sidewalk. Zhemian suddenly saw a piece of extremely exquisite fine tweed hanging in the display window of a tailor shop, and wanted to have a new suit made.

Liu Shan did not express whether she agreed or disagreed with his proposal, so she followed him into the store.

"Okay! Make a suit for me!" The texture was light and the color was good, and Young Master Yu was already satisfied. Without asking the shop assistant for the price, he prepared to pay the deposit.

The shop assistant, with a smile on his face, carefully measured his size with a tape measure. Suddenly, Young Master Yu thought of a question:

"Is this a Chinese product?"

"Yes, the quality is better than foreign goods, and the price is cheaper than foreign goods, sir, I guarantee you'll be satisfied!" the shop assistant replied sincerely.

"Ah! Chinese goods? Unreliable! Unreliable! It wrinkles as soon as you wear it, I don't want it!" Zhemian put the money he had already taken out back into his pocket, indicating that he was determined not to buy it!

"But, sir, how do you know if you haven't tried it?" the shop assistant tried his best to persuade him.

"No need to try, it will definitely wrinkle! What good things are there in Chinese goods!" Zhemian criticized extremely arbitrarily. At the same time, he had already taken Liu Shan's arm and intended to leave.

"Zhemian, may I ask what your surname is?" Ms. Liu suddenly asked this strange question.

"Of course my surname is Yu!"

"Surname Yu? Yu is the surname of the Chinese! Why do you change to a surname like "Washington" or "Roosevelt"?"

Ms. Liu's sharp rebuttal had already made Zhemian's face turn red, but the shop assistants were smiling triumphantly.

"Surname Yu? You are Chinese! Why don't you love Chinese goods? Why do you hate Chinese goods for no reason, you poor piece of subjugated slave material!" Ms. Liu hated him extremely. She felt that Zhemian's actions today had clearly proven that he had no sincerity in accepting the various exhortations she had given him on weekdays. She couldn't help but feel infinitely indignant, scolded a few sentences, and left angrily. The next day, Ms. Liu resolutely completed the divorce procedures with Young Master Yu, went north alone, and joined the ranks of the battlefield rescue team.

Free Talk

Go to the Countryside! 283

— Cao Juren

My opinion is slightly different from those of Mr. Xuan and Mr. Yang Xingzhi. I am biased towards "going back to the countryside."

There are now three types of countryside in China: (A) The countryside in Henan and Shaanxi has long become "villages without farmers." The county magistrate orders the planting of tobacco, and if you can't pay the tobacco tax, you get beaten. The young masters in the city eat Camel cigarettes, and the big girls in the countryside have no pants to wear. This kind of "village without farmers" is of course impossible to return to. (B) The countryside in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Hunan, and Anhui has big landlords and tenant farmers. Capitalism eats the big landlords, and the big landlords eat the tenant farmers again. This kind of countryside, which is on the verge of collapse, is also impossible to return to. But there is also a third type of countryside in China: (C) The countryside centered on self-cultivating farmers. For example, my hometown, the countryside in the upper reaches of the Qiantang River, has very few wealthy households with more than ten thousand gold. Self-cultivating farmers account for eight out of ten. It is not a utopia, but there is plenty of room for heroes to use their talents. If we can go back, we will absolutely not be disappointed.

What do we do when we return to the countryside? We organize self-cultivating farmers to fight a self-defense war. At present, capitalism has sucked the essence of Type A villages dry, and Type B villages have no sweetness to be had. Only Type C villages are seen as a fat piece of meat, and they want to devour it. If new terms like agricultural electrification become their means of stepping into the countryside, self-cultivating farmers will immediately be trampled under their feet. We must help self-cultivating farmers form strong groups and realize agricultural electrification through collective agricultural groups. If we enable self-cultivating farmers to maintain their own equipment, then capitalism will lose the opportunity to grab it. Once the opportunity turns, Type B villages will also have hope of a turnaround.

The establishment of a new society, no matter what process is used, must be followed by construction after destruction. Increasing the strength of Type C villages is laying the cornerstone for the rural economy. A new society that has escaped from famine will be able to restore its social order quickly, so fighting a self-defense war for self-cultivating farmers is fighting a self-defense war for a new society. Look at the power that consumer cooperative societies have contributed in the progress of the Soviet revolution. We cannot underestimate the power of Type C villages.

Of course, Type C villages also have gentry and scoundrels, but those are easy to deal with. Gentry and scoundrels need to borrow the tiger's power before they can act. They have no direct power to restrain self-cultivating farmers. If we stand with the self-cultivating farmers, we can win even without fighting.

Finally, I would also like to say two sentences that are close to slogans: (We go back to the countryside! We help self-cultivating farmers!)

Sanzi's Dad 284

— Luo Hong

As soon as Sanzi opened his eyes, he saw his dad just getting out of bed, holding a belt in his hand, his upper body still naked, and his blue cloth coat wrapped around the mat. He didn't know when his dad had come back last night. He fell asleep as soon as he lay down on the bed every day, and wouldn't wake up until dawn. Sanzi rubbed his eyes and got out of bed.

"This, you take it out today and paste it on the wall, throw it on the street, or in people's houses, whatever." Dad took out a stack of paper printed with words from under the mat. "Dad, is this what you said, the newspaper you guys made yourselves?"

"No, you put it under the oil paper in the basket, and don't let strangers see it."

Sanzi carried the basket of sesame cakes and fried dough sticks and walked to the open space near the train station. Five or six children had already arrived before him. They met in this place every day. None of those five or six children had a home. Some were because their dads had been crushed to death by machines in the factory. Some had collapsed and died on the road from pulling carts in the hot weather, and their mothers couldn't survive, so they abandoned their children and ran away, and some had committed suicide. Sanzi walked closer to them, lifted a corner of the oil paper in the basket, told them what his dad had said, and gave them a little bit each.

"Sanzi, we'll tell you something," Agou said quietly, making a funny face. "The son of the Zhang boss in that big Western-style house we talked about the other day, we plan to get him."

Little black faces were flashing with light, and they scattered. Sanzi carried the basket and walked the slowest. In his heart, he hoped that his dad would have this kind of thing for him to do again. He had many companions and would definitely do a good job.

Sanzi was really happy today. The thing his dad wanted him to do was really done well. And the sun hadn't reached the feet of the man who smoked every day on that big wall, and he had sold out his basket of sesame cakes and fried dough sticks. Counting it up, he also walked a lot less distance than usual. He hated the scorching sun the most.

Full of joy, he took a big step and turned a corner, but a rickshaw quickly bumped into him. He didn't have time to dodge, and the wheel had already crushed his toes. He was about to curse when he heard someone say, "Sanzi, why are you running so fast?" As soon as he heard the voice, he knew that the rickshaw puller was also his companion, Xiao Er. He quickly turned his head to look, and he was right. A pretty woman was sitting in the rickshaw, and the woman was holding a pretty little umbrella. He looked at Xiao Er's back and felt that he was luckier to sell sesame cakes than him.

He went home so happily. But his dad didn't come back that day. The next morning, as soon as he opened his eyes, he was the only one in the room. He went to ask the dad of Little Qizi next door. This man with a face full of black moles told him that his dad had been arrested by the police.

Sanzi's dad never came back from then on.

The Rice-Bowl-Eating Knives 285

— Li

In Jinhua, besides the eight classes of people—Party members, clergy, officials, farmers, laborers, merchants, students, and soldiers—there is also a special class who “eat rice with knives.” Those who "eat rice with knives" are all good fellows, eating well and dressing well, burning incense and worshiping deities, with a group of heroes as their comrades. These heroes and good fellows: those residents who obey them prosper, and those who defy them perish. In the past, those who "eat rice with knives" first had to kill without batting an eye. Second, they had to be killed without begging for mercy. The most important condition was that when angered, they would draw a snow-white knife and cut off a large piece of flesh from their own body, without even wrinkling their brows, wiping away blood, or uttering a single word of pain. In this way, once the qualifications for "eating rice with knives" were met, they could run rampant at will and be revered even after death. However, in recent years, such good fellows have become rare.

Nowadays, although these fellows still kill without batting an eye, they would never do the foolish thing of cutting off their own flesh, and they would certainly beg for mercy if they were about to be killed. The shortcut to "eating rice with knives" nowadays is first to desperately curry favor with the boss. Second, to flaunt their power against those weaker than themselves, and to be extremely cautious towards those stronger than themselves. Once these two conditions are met, they can then attach themselves to a wealthy gentleman, and for a reward of fifty or eighty dollars, go and kill a foolish person who is without wealth or courage and has unfortunately offended the wealthy gentleman.

It is said that the highest reward goes to those who can inflict ten or eight knife wounds, crippling a person so that they wish they could neither live nor die. Next is those who can inflict five or six knife wounds, rendering a person unable to speak or move their hands, writhing in a pool of blood, and dying after several days. The lowest reward goes to those who stab once, causing instant death, allowing the victim to die quickly and painlessly.

Valuing money and devaluing friendship, those who "eat rice with knives," although belonging to the proletariat, have wealthy masters, and their consciousness is the same as that of the propertied class, utterly disliking the poor, so they will not rebel.

Those who "eat rice with knives" are very useful to a group of wealthy gentlemen. Therefore, they are heroes.

Bitter Smiles, Groans, and Cries 286

— Ba Jin

丨To My Brother丨

Your train leaves at seven o'clock, and I left the platform before six thirty. It wasn't because I was afraid of missing the Pukou ferry, as that small steamer doesn't leave until seven twenty. You may have noticed that when leaving, I only shook your hand loosely and gave a faint smile before turning away. I didn't look back at you even once. But after leaving the station, I was unwilling to head towards the river. Hui and I walked slowly along that long corridor, walking back and forth several times without saying a word to each other. Suddenly, the sharp sound of a train whistle pierced my ears, followed by the sound of train wheels moving. I knew you were starting your journey north. Your gaunt face appeared vaguely before my eyes, and my heart began to ache faintly. I didn't shed tears, but my voice was already somewhat hoarse.

"(Let's go)," Hui urged, his voice sounding the same as mine. And so, we left Pukou. Thus, the past ten days of life completely disappeared behind us, and I felt as if I had awakened from a long dream.

You are returning to Tianjin. Before you boarded the train, others said that place was somewhat dangerous, advising you not to return there, but I didn't say a single word of dissuasion. It wasn't that I was unaware of the changes in the so-called anti-Japanese military situation these past few days, nor that I wasn't concerned about your safety. But I knew something else even better: you, like me, are destined to struggle in danger and hardship, and you have neither the opportunity nor the right to seek an easy life. The burden of life weighs upon your youthful shoulders, and a monthly salary of eighty yuan buys all your time. You have no freedom of thought, let alone freedom of action. From our conversations over the past ten days, I have already understood the entirety of your mundane and painful life.

Of course, you had two experiences like this the year before last. You yourself cannot fail to know that the place you are going to will change its colors very quickly, and perhaps you will even be forced to change your nationality there. But what can you do? In the name of prolonged resistance, people are breaking records for losing territory, people are shipping paintings and calligraphy overseas, people are moving antiques, people are levying aviation donations from you, people are announcing victory news in the newspapers every day, people are advocating "(aviation to save the nation)," "(dancing to save the nation)," "(entertainment to save the nation)," "(love to save the nation)," people, when not serving the Party and the nation, are gambling and playing with prostitutes, people... but you have to return to that place that is about to be abandoned for a monthly salary of eighty yuan.

"(What else can be done)?" There must be great sorrow hidden in the words you uttered with a smile. When you think of the things above, your heart must ache with grief and indignation, but if you think further, remembering the tens of thousands of people in that area who have been forgotten by the prolonged resistance and are groaning and struggling under guns and bombs, you may feel that your own fate is not so miserable after all. Perhaps you will even abandon your mundane and painful life and throw yourself into their midst to do something for them. I think you will do this, because I saw that when you talked about the tens of thousands of people groaning and struggling under the iron hooves, your face, which had been ravaged by life, suddenly glowed, and your weary body suddenly filled with vitality. I know now what can still stir your weakening heart. But I am afraid, I am afraid that another big blow will shatter you completely. (To be continued)

Carrot Top 287

— By Jules Renard, Translated by Lin Qu

Chamber Pot (1)

Having made a mess in bed more than once, Carrot Top was very careful to take precautions every night. In summer, this was easy. At nine o'clock, when the Lepic family sent Carrot Top to bed, he would willingly go out for a stroll; and the night would pass without incident.

In winter, however, this walk became a chore. As soon as it got dark, he would take his first precaution when going to shut up the chickens, but this would not last until the next morning. After dinner, and a little more idle time, it was already nine o'clock, and it had been dark for a long time, and this darkness would continue endlessly. Carrot Top had to take a second precaution.

This evening, like many evenings before, he was considering.

"(Do I need to)?" he thought; "(or don't I need to)?"

Usually, either because there was indeed no room for retreat, or because the bright moonlight had bolstered his courage, he would always answer "(yes)." Occasionally, Lepic and his elder brother Felix also served as examples for him. Moreover, his need did not always force him to go far from home, to the ditch almost beside the road in the wilderness. Usually, he would mostly stop under the stairs; this depended on the nature of his need.

But tonight, dense raindrops sifted the windowpane, the wind had extinguished the starlight, and the walnut tree roared angrily in the pasture.

"(It doesn't feel like much)," Carrot Top concluded after careful consideration, "(I don't need to)."

After saying goodnight to everyone, he lit a candle and ran to his desolate and lonely room at the end of the corridor on the right. He took off his clothes, lay in bed, and waited for the Lepic family to come in to check on him. She tightened the blankets and blew out the candle in one go. She left him the candle, but not a single match. Then she locked him in the room, locking the door with a key from the outside. 丨丨 This was because he was afraid of the dark. Carrot Top initially savored the pleasure of being alone in the room. He enjoyed thinking in the darkness. He recalled the events of the day, he was glad he had safely escaped many difficulties, and he hoped to have the same luck again tomorrow. He hoped that for two days in a row, the Lepic family would not notice him, and he wanted to fall asleep peacefully with this fantasy.

He had just closed his eyes when he felt an unpleasantness he had experienced before.

"(This was inevitable)," Carrot Top thought to himself.

Others would get up at this time. But Carrot Top knew there was no chamber pot under the bed. Although the Lepic family would swear and deny it, she always forgot to give him a chamber pot. And since Carrot Top had already taken precautions, what use would a chamber pot be?

So Carrot Top, at the very moment he should have gotten up, continued to speculate.

"(Sooner or later I will have to give in)," he thought in his heart. "(The more I endure, the more I accumulate. But if I release it immediately, I will only release a little bit, and my body temperature will have time to dry the blankets. Based on experience, I am absolutely certain that Mom won't notice at all)."

Carrot Top alleviated his discomfort, very peacefully closed his eyes again, and began to fall asleep.
